- doctrine: `wanting-more-than-your-allotment-is-sin` (vv3-6 тАФ Mosiah 4:27 from inside) ┬╖ `God-grants-according-to-desire` (vv4-5) ┬╖ `God-teaches-every-nation-in-its-own-tongue` (v8 тАФ 5:21-adjacent) ┬╖ theme: `scale-ambition-to-one-soul-through-your-calling` (vv6-9) ┬╖ `joy-fuller-in-others-success` (vv14-16)

### from Alma 30 (Korihor the anti-Christ)
- person: `Korihor` (anti-Christ; full secular-materialist creed; struck dumb; "I always knew"; trodden down) ┬╖ `Alma-the-younger` (refutes by argument first, sign last; discerns willful unbelief) ┬╖ `Giddonah` (high priest at Gideon)
- doctrine: `no-law-against-belief-punish-crimes-not-faith` (vv7-11) ┬╖ `all-things-denote-there-is-a-God` (v44 тАФ design argument) ┬╖ `argument-before-sign-reason-first` (vv37-47) ┬╖ `unbelief-as-chosen-lie-believed-through-success` (vv42, 52-53) ┬╖ theme: `the-complete-anti-Christ-creed` (vv13-18) ┬╖ `accusation-by-projection-priestcraft` (vv27-35) ┬╖ `the-devil-abandons-his-children` (v60)

### from Alma 31 (the Rameumptom тАФ false worship)
- person: `the-Zoramites-Zoram` (dissenters; Rameumptom worship; deny Christ; elect-by-pride) ┬╖ `Alma-the-younger` (heartbroken; prays for strength + the lost) ┬╖ place: `Rameumptom` (the high one-man stand)
- theme: `false-worship-as-inversion-of-true` (vv12-23) ┬╖ `the-two-prayers-self-vs-others` (vv16-18 vs 30-35) ┬╖ doctrine: `election-by-pride-vs-mercy` (vv16-18, 24-25) ┬╖ `the-word-more-powerful-than-the-sword` (v5) ┬╖ `affliction-swallowed-in-the-joy-of-Christ` (vv36-38)

### from Alma 32 (the seed тАФ faith as experiment)
- person: `Alma-the-younger` (faith sermon; reads the poor's affliction as preparation) ┬╖ `the-poor-cast-out` (barred for apparel; humbled, ready)
- doctrine: `faith-is-hope-in-unseen-things-which-are-true` (v21) ┬╖ `the-entry-bar-is-only-desire` (v27) ┬╖ `the-seed-experiment` (vv28-35 тАФ discernible light) ┬╖ `experimental-knowledge-of-that-thing-not-all` (v34) ┬╖ `faith-must-be-nourished-or-it-withers` (vv37-41) ┬╖ `compelled-vs-voluntary-humility` (vv13-16) ┬╖ theme: `worship-not-confined-to-building-or-week` (vv10-11) ┬╖ `the-word-comes-through-the-overlooked` (v23 тАФ men, women, children)

### from Alma 33 (Zenos, worship everywhere, the brazen serpent)
- person: `Zenos` (lost prophet; worship-everywhere prayer; mercy "because of thy Son") ┬╖ `Zenock` (lost prophet; testified of the Son; stoned) ┬╖ `Moses-brazen-serpent` (the type raised in the wilderness)
- doctrine: `worship-is-bound-to-no-place` (vv3-11) ┬╖ `every-mercy-is-because-of-the-Son` (v11) ┬╖ `the-scandal-of-the-simple-look` (vv19-21) ┬╖ `the-seed-is-the-word-of-Christ` (vv22-23) ┬╖ theme: `burdens-made-light-through-the-joy-of-the-Son` (v23)

### from Alma 34 (Amulek тАФ infinite atonement, mercy + justice, "this life is the time")
- person: `Amulek` (atonement sermon; personal testimony; hypocrisy rebuke)
- doctrine: `the-atonement-must-be-infinite` (vv9-14) ┬╖ `mercy-satisfies-justice-encircles-in-safety` (vv15-16 тАФ seed of Alma 42) ┬╖ `the-law-every-whit-points-to-the-sacrifice` (vv13-14) ┬╖ `prayer-without-mercy-to-the-needy-is-hypocrisy` (vv28-29 тАФ "dross" reversed) ┬╖ `this-life-is-the-time-to-prepare` (vv31-33) ┬╖ `the-spirit-you-die-with-persists` (vv34-35) ┬╖ theme: `prayer-everywhere-over-everything-continually` (vv17-27) ┬╖ `dont-let-the-casting-out-make-you-like-them` (vv40-41)

### from Alma 35 (Zoramite block close тАФ refugees become refuge; pivot to the sons)
- person: `the-Zoramite-leaders` (angry the word destroyed their craft; secret purge) ┬╖ `the-people-of-Ammon` (former refugees now shelter cast-out Zoramites) ┬╖ `the-new-Zoramite-converts` (expelled; take up arms тАФ not under the Ammonite oath) ┬╖ `Alma-the-younger` (grieved; pivots to his sons)
- theme: `the-word-destroys-craft` (vv3-6) ┬╖ `the-sheltered-become-shelterers` (vv8-9) ┬╖ `pacifism-was-a-covenant-not-a-blanket-rule` (vv13-14) ┬╖ `offended-by-the-strictness-of-the-word` (v15) ┬╖ `pivot-from-public-mission-to-private-stewardship` (v16 тАФ opens 36-42)

## тАФ ALMA'S COUNSEL TO HIS SONS (36-42) тАФ
*Each charge given "separately" (35:16): Helaman (36-37), Shiblon (38), Corianton (39-42). The book's most personal block тАФ fatherhood after the wide field hardened.*

### from Alma 36 (to Helaman тАФ the conversion told whole, chiastic)
- person: `Alma-the-younger` (conversion paradigm; persecutorтЖТpreacher) ┬╖ `Helaman` (the son receiving the charge)
- structure: `chiasmus-centered-on-the-cry` (vv1-30, pivot vv17-18) ┬╖ doctrine: `pains-of-hell-are-memory-in-Gods-presence` (vv13-16) ┬╖ `a-different-memory-is-the-rescue` (v17) ┬╖ `the-cry-stripped-to-the-name-and-mercy` (v18) ┬╖ `joy-exactly-as-deep-as-the-pain` (vv20-21) ┬╖ `conversion-becomes-vocation` (v24) ┬╖ `reproducible-conversion-tasted-eye-to-eye` (v26) ┬╖ event: `longing-replaces-the-wish-to-be-banished` (vv15, 22)

### from Alma 37 (to Helaman cont. тАФ records, small means, the Liahona)
- person: `Alma-the-younger` ┬╖ `Helaman` (entrusted with records + interpreters) ┬╖ object: `the-sacred-records-Liahona-24-plates`
- doctrine: `by-small-and-simple-things` (vv6-7) ┬╖ `scriptures-preserve-memory-and-convert` (vv8-9) ┬╖ `teach-the-fruit-of-evil-not-the-recipe` (vv21-32) ┬╖ `counsel-with-the-Lord-in-all-thy-doings` (vv35-37) ┬╖ `the-Liahona-as-type-of-the-word` (vv38-46) ┬╖ theme: `the-failure-is-despising-the-easy-way` (vv41, 46)

### from Alma 38 (to Shiblon тАФ the steady son)
- person: `Shiblon` (steady, faithful; suffered among the Zoramites; receives approval) ┬╖ `Alma-the-younger`
- doctrine: `bridle-passions-that-ye-may-be-filled-with-love` (v12 тАФ restraint as precondition for love) ┬╖ `no-other-way-but-Christ` (v9) ┬╖ `conversion-is-pain-until-the-cry-then-peace` (vv6-8) ┬╖ theme: `three-sons-three-different-words` (vv2-3) ┬╖ `inoculate-the-faithful-son-against-pride` (vv11-14 тАФ publican vs Rameumptom)

### from Alma 39 (to Corianton тАФ the grieved father confronts)
- person: `Corianton` (strayed тАФ boasted, forsook ministry, went after Isabel) ┬╖ `Alma-the-younger` (rebuke framed by love) ┬╖ `Isabel` (the harlot at Siron)
- doctrine: `the-sin-started-in-pride-not-appetite` (v2) ┬╖ `sexual-sin-ranks-third-because-of-the-power-it-misuses` (vv5-6) ┬╖ `the-representatives-sin-costs-others-their-belief` (v11) ┬╖ `repentance-includes-restitution-and-counsel` (vv10-13) ┬╖ theme: `harrowing-the-soul-for-its-good` (vv7-8) ┬╖ `rebuild-the-belief-under-the-behavior` (vv15-19 тЖТ 40-42)

### from Alma 40 (the resurrection тАФ answer to the worried son)
- person: `Alma-the-younger` (revelation-vs-opinion honesty) ┬╖ `Corianton` (worried about the resurrection)
- doctrine: `the-space-and-the-intermediate-state` (vv11-14 тАФ paradise/rest, outer darkness/fearful-looking-for) ┬╖ `the-resurrection-restores-the-perfect-frame` (v23 тАФ not a hair lost) ┬╖ `resurrection-certain-the-floor-under-repentance` (vv4-21) ┬╖ `universal-resurrection-divergent-destinies` (vv25-26) ┬╖ theme: `prophetic-intellectual-honesty-revelation-vs-opinion` (vv5, 20) ┬╖ `resurrection-makes-mortality-matter-forever` (vv21, 26)

### from Alma 41 (the restoration тАФ "wickedness never was happiness")
- person: `Corianton` (wrested "restoration" into self-justifying universalism) ┬╖ `Alma-the-younger`
- doctrine: `wickedness-never-was-happiness` (vv10-11 тАФ contradictory natures) ┬╖ `restoration-is-reciprocity-not-reset` (vv12-13) ┬╖ `you-are-restored-to-the-self-your-desires-built` (vv3-7) ┬╖ `what-you-send-out-returns` (vv14-15) ┬╖ theme: `bad-theology-cleared-the-way-for-bad-behavior` (vv1, 9) ┬╖ `the-doctrine-condemns-the-unrepentant-and-saves-the-repentant` (v15)

### from Alma 42 (justice & mercy тАФ the Corianton block climax)
- person: `Corianton` (denied God's justice to excuse his sin) ┬╖ `Alma-the-younger`
- doctrine: `the-expulsion-was-mercy-it-created-the-space-to-repent` (vv2-7) ┬╖ `law-punishment-repentance-chain` (vv16-22) ┬╖ `God-himself-pays-justice-so-mercy-can-act` (v15) ┬╖ `mercy-cannot-rob-justice` (vv23-25) ┬╖ `two-kinds-of-trouble-destructive-vs-redemptive` (v29) ┬╖ theme: `attacking-Gods-justice-to-excuse-oneself` (vv1, 30) ┬╖ `repentance-is-the-start-of-the-real-ministry` (v31)

## тАФ THE WAR CHAPTERS (43-62) тАФ
*Captain Moroni; the title of liberty (46); Moroni's character (48); the Amalickiah/Ammoron wars; Helaman's stripling warriors (53, 56-58); the Moroni-Pahoran epistles (60-61). The gospel under siege тАФ liberty, covenant, and faith tested by war.*

### from Alma 43 (Captain Moroni тАФ the better cause)
- person: `Captain-Moroni` (chief captain at 25; armor, revelation, stratagem, mercy) ┬╖ `Zerahemnah` (Lamanite commander; apostate captains preserve hatred) ┬╖ `Lehi-captain` (encircling army at Sidon) ┬╖ `Alma-the-younger` (consulted for strategy)
- doctrine: `the-better-cause-defensive-not-conquest` (vv45-47) ┬╖ `the-law-of-war-bear-the-offense-then-defend` (vv46-47 тАФ D&C 98) ┬╖ theme: `Moroni-prepares-armor-as-a-moral-act` (vv18-21, 37-38) ┬╖ `revelation-and-strategy-together` (vv23-24, 30) ┬╖ `mercy-in-victory-stop-when-the-threat-is-contained` (v54) ┬╖ `dissenters-drive-the-war` (vv6-8)

### from Alma 44 (Zerahemnah surrenders тАФ conditional protection)
- person: `Captain-Moroni` (conditional-protection doctrine; keeps his word; repeated mercy) ┬╖ `Zerahemnah` (credits armor not God; refuses then accepts the oath; scalped)
- doctrine: `conditional-protection-faithful-or-fall` (v4) ┬╖ theme: `two-readings-of-the-same-victory` (vv3 vs 9 тАФ providence vs armor) ┬╖ `Moronis-word-binds-him` (vv10-11) ┬╖ `mercy-with-a-limit-spare-the-person-not-the-threat` (vv6, 11) ┬╖ `repeated-mercy-stop-the-killing-when-the-enemy-yields` (v20) ┬╖ event: `end-of-Almas-record` (v24)

### from Alma 45 (Alma's prophecy + departure тАФ Helaman's record begins)
- person: `Alma-the-younger` (final prophecy, blessing, translation-like departure) ┬╖ `Helaman` (reaffirms belief; receives records; takes up ministry)
- prophecy: `Nephite-extinction-400-years` (vv10-14) ┬╖ event: `Almas-translation-like-departure` (vv18-19 тАФ "even as Moses") ┬╖ doctrine: `the-conditional-land-covenant` (v16) ┬╖ theme: `the-prophecy-sealed-until-fulfilled` (v9) ┬╖ `the-pride-cycle-reignites-the-moment-deliverance-passes` (vv1, 23-24) ┬╖ `Mormon-lives-the-fulfillment-he-records` (vv10-14)

### from Alma 46 (the title of liberty)
- person: `Amalickiah` (the flatterer; cunning + flattering words; bids for kingship) ┬╖ `Captain-Moroni` (rends coat into title of liberty; prays before proclaiming) ┬╖ object: `the-title-of-liberty` ("our God, our religion, and freedom, and our peace, our wives, and our children")
- doctrine: `the-inner-threat-of-flattery-and-ambition` (vv4-10) ┬╖ `the-self-maledictory-covenant-of-liberty` (vv19-22) ┬╖ `conditional-protection-destroyed-only-by-our-transgressions` (v18) ┬╖ theme: `how-quick-to-forget-after-deliverance` (vv7-8) ┬╖ `prayer-before-the-banner` (v13) ┬╖ `the-Joseph-remnant-typology-refuses-to-flatter` (vv23-27) ┬╖ `the-hard-edge-of-wartime-liberty` (v35) ┬╖ event: `Christians-named` (vv14-15)

### from Alma 47 (Amalickiah's treachery тАФ "come down from the mount")
- person: `Amalickiah` (master of treachery; flatteryтЖТcommandтЖТbetrayalтЖТpoisonтЖТmurderтЖТthrone) ┬╖ `Lehonti` (lured off the mount, poisoned by degrees) ┬╖ `the-Lamanite-king` (trusts the token of peace, stabbed)
- theme: `come-down-from-the-mount` (vv7-13 тАФ lured off secure ground) ┬╖ `poison-by-degrees` (v18) ┬╖ `treachery-weaponizes-trust` (vv10-35) ┬╖ `accuse-the-innocent-of-your-own-crime` (vv24-30) ┬╖ `Amalickiah-as-anti-Moroni` (secrecy/fraud vs transparency/prayer) ┬╖ doctrine: `apostate-worse-strange-to-relate` (v36)

### from Alma 48 (the portrait of Moroni)
- person: `Captain-Moroni` (fullest character portrait тАФ greatness of character not capacity) ┬╖ `Amalickiah` (power by fraud, the foil) ┬╖ `Helaman-the-preachers` ("no less serviceable")
- theme: `greatness-is-character-not-capacity` (v7) ┬╖ `the-general-and-the-preacher-are-equals` (vv18-19) ┬╖ `the-reluctant-warrior-grieves-the-unprepared-dead` (vv23-24) ┬╖ `competence-in-service-of-love-not-the-reverse` (vv11-13) ┬╖ doctrine: `if-all-men-were-like-Moroni-hell-would-be-shaken` (v17) ┬╖ `the-Nephite-war-faith-defense-never-offense` (vv14-16)

### from Alma 49 (fortified cities tested тАФ preparation pays off)
- person: `Captain-Moroni` (fortifies the weak city most; anticipates enemy's logic) ┬╖ `Amalickiah` (curses God + Moroni for the faithfulness that beat him) ┬╖ `Lehi-captain` (commands Noah; feared) ┬╖ `Corianton` (restored, now preaching)
- theme: `preparation-defeats-numbers-and-is-how-God-works` (vv2-23) ┬╖ `anticipate-the-enemys-logic-fortify-the-weak-point-most` (vv14-15) ┬╖ `two-responses-to-one-deliverance` (vv27-28) ┬╖ `Amalickiah-hates-God-because-faithfulness-works` (v27) ┬╖ event: `Corianton-restored-among-the-preachers` (v30)

### from Alma 50 (expansion, prosperity, Morianton)
- person: `Captain-Moroni` (fortifies all cities; happiest-time era) ┬╖ `Morianton` ("man of much passion"; undone by beating a maidservant) ┬╖ `the-maidservant` (abused, exposes the plan, saves the nation) ┬╖ `Teancum` (introduced; slays Morianton) ┬╖ `Pahoran-Nephihah` (righteous chief judges)
- doctrine: `the-Lehi-covenant-verified-as-historical-law` (vv19-22) ┬╖ theme: `the-happiest-time-was-readiness-plus-faithfulness` (v23) ┬╖ `private-cruelty-betrays-the-public-scheme` (vv30-31) ┬╖ `the-overlooked-person-is-the-hinge` (v31) ┬╖ reference: `the-oath-of-good-governance` (vv37-40)

### from Alma 51 (king-men + Amalickiah's death)
- person: `the-king-men` (high-birth faction seeking monarchy; seditious in defeat) ┬╖ `the-freemen-Pahoran` (free government by the voice of the people) ┬╖ `Captain-Moroni` (crushes internal sedition) ┬╖ `Amalickiah` (dies by Teancum's javelin asleep) ┬╖ `Teancum` (the night raid)
- theme: `sedition-born-from-factional-spite` (v13) ┬╖ `internal-division-opens-the-door-to-conquest` (vv22-27) ┬╖ `the-nations-own-fortifications-turned-against-it` (v27) ┬╖ `the-hard-edge-of-wartime-sedition-law` (vv15-21) ┬╖ `the-pit-digger-falls-into-his-own-pit` (vv9-10, 33-37)

### from Alma 52 (Ammoron + Mulek retaken by decoy)
- person: `Ammoron` (Amalickiah's brother; inherits throne + war) ┬╖ `Captain-Moroni` (the decoy; mercy in the trap; wounded) ┬╖ `Teancum` (the bait force) ┬╖ `Lehi-captain` (the fresh pincer) ┬╖ `Jacob-Zoramite` (fights to the death; killed)
- theme: `organized-evil-outlives-its-leader` (vv3-4) ┬╖ `dont-fight-on-the-enemys-terms` (vv5, 17) ┬╖ `the-decoy-and-the-pincer` (vv21-31 тАФ ambush of Ai) ┬╖ `mercy-maximizes-surrenders-not-kills` (vv37-40) ┬╖ `the-dissenters-ferocity-destroys-him` (vv33-40)

### from Alma 53 (the stripling warriors rise)
- person: `the-people-of-Ammon` (covenant-keepers; want to break the oath out of love, restrained) ┬╖ `Helaman` (restrains the fathers; leads the 2000 sons) ┬╖ `the-two-thousand-stripling-warriors` (sons not under the oath; faithfulness their defining trait) ┬╖ `Captain-Moroni-Lehi` (prisoner-wall)
- doctrine: `keeping-the-covenant-while-watching-others-bleed-for-it` (vv13-15) ┬╖ `faithfulness-true-in-whatsoever-entrusted-is-the-defining-trait` (vv20-21) ┬╖ theme: `the-next-generation-takes-up-what-the-parents-could-not` (vv16-18) ┬╖ `internal-dissension-costs-ground-again` (vv8-9) ┬╖ `the-captives-build-their-own-prison-wall` (vv4-5)

### from Alma 54 (Moroni-Ammoron letters)
- person: `Captain-Moroni` (letter grounded in God/justice/repentance + honest anger) ┬╖ `Ammoron` (letter grounded in grievance/revenge/agnostic evasion)
- theme: `two-foundations-conscience-vs-grievance` (whole ch) ┬╖ `agnosticism-as-moral-evasion` (vv21-22) ┬╖ `the-tell-of-half-belief` (v22) ┬╖ `grievance-mutated-into-a-political-claim` (vv17, 24) ┬╖ `the-borrowed-grievance` (vv23-24 тАФ Zoramite wearing Lamanite grievance) ┬╖ `honest-anger-vs-cold-dismissal` (vv13, 22)

### from Alma 55 (Gid taken without blood)
- person: `Captain-Moroni` (bloodless victory; refuses to kill the helpless) ┬╖ `Laman-Nephite-scout` (executes the wine stratagem) ┬╖ `Ammoron` (knows his cause unjust, fights anyway)
- doctrine: `refusing-to-kill-the-helpless-even-when-you-could` (vv18-19 тАФ David/sleeping-Saul) ┬╖ theme: `the-stratagem-that-serves-mercy` (vv4-24) ┬╖ `the-enemys-own-appetite-is-the-weapon` (vv10-14) ┬╖ `angriest-at-the-knowingly-false` (v1) ┬╖ `remember-God-and-dont-fall-for-your-own-trick` (vv30-32)

### from Alma 56 (Helaman's epistle тАФ the stripling warriors fight)
- person: `Helaman` (writes epistle; leads + protects the 2000 "sons") ┬╖ `the-two-thousand-stripling-warriors` (fearless faith; none slain) ┬╖ `the-mothers-of-Ammon` (taught "if ye doubt not, God will deliver") ┬╖ `Antipus` (commander; falls, "happy")
- doctrine: `faith-taught-by-believing-mothers` (v47) ┬╖ `believing-on-the-words-of-a-trusted-witness` (v48 тАФ "we do not doubt our mothers knew it") ┬╖ theme: `courage-that-is-a-function-of-faith-not-bravado` (vv45-47) ┬╖ `reluctance-even-in-the-young-warriors` (v46) ┬╖ event: `not-one-of-the-two-thousand-slain` (vv55-56)

### from Alma 57 (campaign continues тАФ exactness + the deepened miracle)
- person: `Helaman` (counts the wounded) ┬╖ `the-two-thousand-and-sixty-stripling-warriors` (exact obedience; all wounded, none slain) ┬╖ `Gid` (prisoner-guard; reports the rebellion)
- doctrine: `obedience-with-exactness-as-the-form-of-faith` (v21) ┬╖ `faith-preserves-through-the-wounds-not-from-them` (vv25-26) ┬╖ `preservation-is-a-particular-sign-not-a-universal-rule` (vv26, 36) ┬╖ theme: `minds-firm-trust-continually` (v27) ┬╖ `the-honest-horror-of-even-a-righteous-war` (vv14, 32-33 тАФ surrendered prisoners slain in rebellion)

### from Alma 58 (siege of Manti тАФ peace to the soul; refuse to murmur)
- person: `Helaman` (receives peace; refuses to murmur when abandoned) ┬╖ `Gid-Teomner` (the ambush that takes Manti) ┬╖ `the-stripling-warriors` (stand fast; none slain)
- doctrine: `God-speaks-peace-to-the-soul-before-the-deliverance` (vv10-11) ┬╖ `peace-and-faith-are-the-strengthening-not-a-consolation-prize` (vv11-12) ┬╖ theme: `refuse-to-murmur-when-your-own-side-fails-you` (vv34-37) ┬╖ `Helaman-vs-Moroni-two-responses-to-neglect` (vv35-37 vs ch 60) ┬╖ `wisdom-adapts-against-a-learning-enemy` (vv1, 13-28) ┬╖ `preservation-was-the-sign-daily-faithfulness-the-substance` (vv39-40)

### from Alma 59 (Nephihah falls тАФ Moroni's anger kindles)
- person: `Captain-Moroni` (rejoices, then doubts, then angry at the government) ┬╖ `Pahoran` (assumed indifferent тАФ wrongly) ┬╖ `Helaman` (the foil)
- event: `the-fall-of-Nephihah` (vv5-10) ┬╖ doctrine: `prevention-is-cheaper-than-recovery` (v9) ┬╖ theme: `even-Moroni-doubts` (vv11-12) ┬╖ `doubt-curdling-into-anger-at-the-wrong-target` (v13) ┬╖ `judging-a-matter-before-hearing-it` (v13)

### from Alma 60 (Moroni's furious epistle)
- person: `Captain-Moroni` (accusatory letter тАФ right doctrine + heart, wrong judgment) ┬╖ `Pahoran` (accused of "thoughtless stupor"/treason тАФ falsely)
- doctrine: `the-righteous-slain-are-not-lost-and-not-proof-of-their-wickedness` (vv12-13) ┬╖ `death-of-the-righteous-condemns-the-negligent-not-the-dead` (vv10-13) ┬╖ `cleanse-the-inward-vessel-first` (vv23-24) ┬╖ `internal-corruption-defeats-before-the-enemy-does` (vv15-16) ┬╖ `fear-God-not-power-seek-to-pull-power-down` (vv28, 36) ┬╖ theme: `right-doctrine-pure-heart-wrong-judgment-of-a-person` (vv7, 18, 33)

### from Alma 61 (Pahoran's gracious reply)
- person: `Pahoran` (falsely accused, driven out by rebels; responds with grace) ┬╖ `Captain-Moroni` (the accuser whose harsh letter still carried a true word) ┬╖ `the-king-men-rebels` (overthrew Zarahemla, allied with Lamanites)
- doctrine: `receive-false-accusation-by-blessing-the-heart-behind-it` (v9) ┬╖ `a-flawed-message-can-still-carry-a-true-word` (vv19-20) ┬╖ `liberty-subordinated-to-obedience-to-God` (vv12-13) ┬╖ theme: `the-assume-the-best-instinct-vindicated` (vv3-8 тАФ Helaman right, Moroni wrong) ┬╖ `take-the-truth-let-the-tone-go` (vv9, 19-20) ┬╖ `conflict-that-deepens-the-friendship` (vv9, 21)

### from Alma 62 (the war ends; same affliction hardens / softens)
- person: `Captain-Moroni` (retakes the cities; retires in peace to Moronihah) ┬╖ `Pahoran` (restored to the judgment-seat) ┬╖ `Teancum` (kills Ammoron in a final solo raid, slain тАФ "a true friend to liberty") ┬╖ `Helaman` (rebuilds the church; dies in the 35th year)
- doctrine: `the-same-affliction-hardens-some-and-softens-others` (v41 тАФ suffering a catalyst, not a cause) ┬╖ `remembering-is-the-antidote-to-the-pride-cycle` (vv49-50 тАФ prosperity without pride because they remembered) ┬╖ `the-prayers-of-the-righteous-spare-the-many` (v40) ┬╖ theme: `righteous-anger-unbridled-carries-a-cost` (vv35-37 тАФ Teancum dies on anger's errand) ┬╖ `the-great-captain-exits-in-peace-not-glory` (v43) ┬╖ `the-grievance-cure-still-working` (vv27-29 тАФ prisoners become free people of Ammon)

### from Alma 63 (close of the book of Alma тАФ continuity, not climax)
- person: `Shiblon` (the steady, just son; receives the records, confers on Helaman) ┬╖ `Corianton` (the restored son; sails north carrying provisions тАФ laboring, not given the records) ┬╖ `Helaman (son of Helaman)` (receives the records тАФ chain into the book of Helaman) ┬╖ `Captain-Moroni` (dies, one verse) ┬╖ `Hagoth` ("an exceedingly curious man"; ships north) ┬╖ `Moronihah` (defeats the Lamanite incursion)
- doctrine: `the-sacred-record-passes-through-chosen-faithful-hands` (vv1-2, 11-17 тАФ generation to generation, Alma 37 fulfilled) ┬╖ theme: `the-restored-son-serves-the-steady-son-keeps` (vv2, 10) ┬╖ `the-great-are-remembered-by-deeds-not-death-notices` (v3 тАФ Moroni's one-line death) ┬╖ `a-record-honest-about-the-limits-of-its-knowledge` (v8 тАФ "whither she did go we know not")

## тАФ THE BOOK OF HELAMAN (great reversal: righteous Lamanites / wicked Nephites; rise of the Gadianton robbers) тАФ

### from Helaman 1 (peace collapses inward; the secret combination is born)
- person: `Pahoran-the-second` (chief judge, murdered on the judgment-seat) ┬╖ `Paanchi` (seditious brother, executed) ┬╖ `Pacumeni` (third brother, chief judge, slain against the wall) ┬╖ `Kishkumen` (the assassin, founder-figure of the secret band) ┬╖ `Coriantumr` (Nephite dissenter, takes Zarahemla, overextends and is slain) ┬╖ `Tubaloth` (son of Ammoron) ┬╖ `Moronihah`/`Lehi` (cut Coriantumr off, retake Zarahemla)
- doctrine: `the-secret-combination-is-the-anti-covenant` (1:11 тАФ oath sworn in God's name to conceal murder) ┬╖ theme: `the-deadliest-threat-is-internal-not-external` (1:1-18) ┬╖ `complacency-leaves-the-center-undefended` (1:18, 26) ┬╖ `audacity-without-depth-of-position-destroys-itself` (1:22-32) ┬╖ `the-great-reversal-righteous-Lamanites-wicked-Nephites` (book heading)

### from Helaman 2 (Gadianton named; the servant foils the band)
- person: `Helaman (son of Helaman)` (chief judge, assassination target, records the book) ┬╖ `Gadianton` ("expert in many words and in his craft"; the named destroyer of the nation) ┬╖ `Kishkumen` (drawn out and slain by the servant) ┬╖ `the-unnamed-servant-of-Helaman` (infiltrates, learns the sign, kills Kishkumen)
- doctrine: `flattery-and-craft-are-the-combination's-door` (2:4-5 тАФ words before violence) ┬╖ theme: `the-combination's-program-is-to-capture-the-state-for-the-insiders` (2:5) ┬╖ `the-counter-to-the-secret-is-one-faithful-person-who-enters-it` (2:6-9) ┬╖ `anonymous-faithfulness-saves-what-the-named-cannot` (2:6-9) ┬╖ `Mormon-names-the-ending-in-advance` (2:13-14 тАФ the seed that overthrows the whole nation)

### from Helaman 3 (two growths in one season; the word divides the snares; sanctification by yielding)
- person: `Helaman (son of Helaman)` (judge with justice; dies v37) ┬╖ `Nephi (son of Helaman)` (eldest, named for founder; succeeds) ┬╖ `Gadianton` (combinations grow unseen by government, v23)
- doctrine: `the-word-of-God-divides-asunder-the-snares-of-the-devil` (3:29-30 тАФ antidote to the combination's craft) ┬╖ `sanctification-comes-by-yielding-the-heart-to-God` (3:35 тАФ give-away-all-my-sins core) ┬╖ `the-gate-of-heaven-is-open-unto-all-who-will` (3:27-28) ┬╖ theme: `two-growths-in-one-season-rot-and-word` (3:23-26) ┬╖ `persecution-is-the-occasion-of-the-humble's-sanctification` (3:34-35) ┬╖ `pride-enters-the-professors-not-the-church` (3:33) ┬╖ `the-Nephite-end-foretold-they-become-Lamanites` (3:16)

### from Helaman 4 (the fall; left in their own strength)
- person: `Moronihah` (regains half the lands on repentance; can obtain no more) ┬╖ `Nephi and Lehi (sons of Helaman)` (preach + prophesy of the iniquities)
- doctrine: `boast-in-your-own-strength-and-you-are-left-in-it` (4:13 тАФ self-sufficiency granted, found man-for-man insufficient) ┬╖ `the-Spirit-dwells-not-in-unholy-temples` (4:24 тАФ withdrawal as incompatibility) ┬╖ `defeat-is-traced-to-wickedness-not-the-enemy` (4:11, D&C 82:10) ┬╖ `repentance-immediately-restores-prosperity` (4:15) ┬╖ theme: `the-pride-that-destroys-is-the-pride-that-oppresses-the-poor` (4:12) ┬╖ `in-the-space-of-not-many-years` (4:26) ┬╖ `the-reversal-completed-Nephites-as-wicked-as-the-Lamanites` (4:22-26)

### from Helaman 5 (remember, remember; the rock; the prison of fire)
- person: `Nephi (son of Helaman)` (gives up the seat to preach; imprisoned; encircled by fire) ┬╖ `Lehi (son of Helaman)` (co-missionary) ┬╖ `Helaman (father)` (the "remember" / rock-of-the-Redeemer charge) ┬╖ `Aminadab` (dissenter who sees the shining faces, teaches the way out of darkness)
- doctrine: `build-on-the-rock-of-the-Redeemer-and-the-storm-cannot-drag-you-down` (5:12) ┬╖ `Christ-redeems-from-sins-not-in-sins` (5:10 тАФ death of cheap grace) ┬╖ `remembering-is-the-foundation-of-discipleship` (5:6-12 тАФ answer to ch4's fall) ┬╖ `names-are-a-call-to-remember-and-become` (5:6-7) ┬╖ `the-still-voice-of-perfect-mildness-shakes-the-earth` (5:30-31) ┬╖ theme: `the-fire-that-protects-instead-of-burns` (5:23-24, 43-44) ┬╖ `cry-unto-the-voice-until-the-darkness-disperses` (5:41-42) ┬╖ `the-word-recovers-what-the-sword-could-not` (5:50-52)

### from Helaman 6 (reversal complete; secret-combination theology; opposite responses)
- person: `Cezoram` (chief judge murdered on the seat; his son too) ┬╖ `Gadianton`/`Kishkumen` (founders, Satan's instruments) ┬╖ `Satan (the author of all sin)` (the one being behind Eden, Cain, Babel, Jaredites, Gadianton) ┬╖ `Nephi and Lehi (sons of Helaman)`
- doctrine: `the-Spirit-follows-the-heart-not-the-lineage` (6:34-36 тАФ withdraws from the hard, pours on the willing; final answer to 2 Ne 5) ┬╖ `easiness-and-willingness-to-believe-is-the-whole-qualification` (6:36) ┬╖ `secret-combinations-are-Satan's-one-continuous-project` (6:26-30 тАФ author of all sin) ┬╖ theme: `prolonged-prosperity-not-affliction-is-the-occasion-of-the-fall` (6:16-17 тАФ dark twin of 62:41) ┬╖ `same-cancer-opposite-responses-opposite-fates` (6:37-38) ┬╖ `the-combination-offers-escape-from-consequence` (6:21, 24 тАФ inverse of the gospel) ┬╖ `the-combination-builds-a-state-within-the-state` (6:22-24, 39)

## тАФ THE PROPHECY OF NEPHI (Helaman 7-16: Nephi's tower lament тЖТ the murder of the chief judge тЖТ the sealing power тЖТ Samuel the Lamanite) тАФ

### from Helaman 7 (Nephi's tower lament; these are my days)
- person: `Nephi (son of Helaman)` (rejected in the north; pours out his soul on the garden tower; cries repentance)
- theme: `these-are-my-days-faithfulness-in-the-age-you-are-given` (7:7-9) ┬╖ `the-prophet's-grief-becomes-the-sermon` (7:11-15) ┬╖ `forgetting-God-in-the-very-day-of-deliverance` (7:20) ┬╖ `judicial-corruption-when-the-combination-captures-the-courts` (7:4-5) ┬╖ doctrine: `greater-knowledge-greater-accountability` (7:23-24 тАФ the key to the reversal) ┬╖ `God's-forsaking-is-self-caused-by-hardened-hearts` (7:17-18)

### from Helaman 8 (the prophet-chain testimony of Christ; the murder revealed)
- person: `Nephi (son of Helaman)` (recites the prophet-chain; reveals the murder) ┬╖ `the Gadianton judges` (incite the crowd; fear the people not God) ┬╖ `the faithful remnant` ("let this man alone... he is a good man")
- doctrine: `all-the-prophets-testified-of-Christ` (8:13-23 тАФ scripture is one testimony) ┬╖ `look-upon-the-Son-of-God-and-live` (8:14-15 тАФ brazen serpent, the simple gaze) ┬╖ `fulfilled-prophecy-is-evidence-for-prophecy-not-yet-fulfilled` (8:20-21 тАФ Mulekites as proof) ┬╖ `unbelief-against-total-evidence-is-willful-not-honest` (8:24) ┬╖ theme: `corruption-fears-the-people-not-God-and-acts-through-the-mob` (8:4-7) ┬╖ `brother-kills-brother-for-the-seat-Cain-runs-again` (8:27-28)

### from Helaman 9 (the murder mystery; Seantum named by sign)
- person: `Nephi (son of Helaman)` (accused of conspiracy; vindicated by the sign; deflects glory to God) ┬╖ `the five` (verify, jailed as murderers, converted in prison) ┬╖ `Seantum` (the fratricide; confesses by the sign) ┬╖ `the Gadianton judges` (invent the conspiracy theory; bribe + threaten)
- theme: `overwhelming-evidence-met-with-a-manufactured-alternative` (9:16 тАФ motivated unbelief) ┬╖ doctrine: `true-prophecy-is-specific-and-falsifiable` (9:25-37 тАФ the step-by-step Seantum sign) ┬╖ `the-faithful-messenger-deflects-glory-to-God` (9:36) ┬╖ theme: `the-crowd-deifies-the-messenger` (9:41 тАФ the error Nephi forestalled) ┬╖ `the-corrupt-assume-everyone-has-a-price` (9:20 тАФ the bribe) ┬╖ `judgment-by-appearance-convicts-the-innocent` (9:6-9)

### from Helaman 10 (the sealing power given)
- person: `Nephi (son of Helaman)` (given the sealing power in the valley; turns straight back to preach; carried by the Spirit)
- doctrine: `the-condition-of-unlimited-power-is-a-will-that-will-not-ask-amiss` (10:5 тАФ the blank check made safe) ┬╖ `the-sealing-power-bind-and-loose-on-earth-and-in-heaven` (10:7, Matt 16:19) ┬╖ `unwearyingness-is-the-commended-virtue` (10:4-5) ┬╖ theme: `the-blessing-comes-in-the-valley-not-the-mountaintop` (10:2-4) ┬╖ `the-power-serves-the-ministry-not-the-prophet` (10:11-12) ┬╖ `thou-art-Nephi-and-I-am-God-the-line-that-humbles-and-protects` (10:6 тАФ corrects the ch9 deification)

### from Helaman 11 (a famine instead of the sword; the cycle in fast-forward)
- person: `Nephi (son of Helaman)` (asks the famine; prays back the rain) ┬╖ `Lehi (his brother)` ("not a whit behind him")
- doctrine: `the-prophet-asks-for-affliction-as-mercy` (11:4 тАФ famine not sword) ┬╖ `affliction-drives-to-remembrance-where-the-word-could-not` (11:7) ┬╖ `real-repentance-sweeps-the-cancer-away-not-just-the-consequence` (11:10) ┬╖ `the-intercessor-reasons-from-God's-own-promise` (11:14-16) ┬╖ theme: `the-pride-cycle-in-fast-forward` (11:1-37) ┬╖ `the-tragedy-of-temporary-remembrance` (11:36 тАФ "again" they forget) ┬╖ `the-combination-cannot-be-defeated-by-force-alone` (11:28-33)

### from Helaman 12 (Mormon's great lament on the human heart)
- person: `Mormon (narrator)` (the editorial meditation)
- doctrine: `man-is-less-than-the-dust-because-the-dust-obeys` (12:7-8 тАФ the cutting nothingness) ┬╖ `prosperity-is-the-moment-of-forgetting` (12:2) ┬╖ `chastening-is-the-only-reliable-teacher-of-the-forgetful-heart` (12:3 тАФ the "why affliction" capstone) ┬╖ `the-heart's-asymmetry-quick-to-evil-slow-to-good` (12:4-5) ┬╖ `the-root-rebellion-is-not-wanting-God-to-rule` (12:6 тАФ inverse of Nephi's surrendered will 10:5) ┬╖ `the-creation-obeys-God's-voice-instantly` (12:8-17, incl. heliocentric aside v15) ┬╖ `repentance-was-declared-that-men-might-be-saved` (12:22 тАФ door after the doom)

## тАФ THE PROPHECY OF SAMUEL THE LAMANITE (Helaman 13-15: the outsider prophet on the wall; the signs of Christ's birth + death; the great reversal preached) тАФ

### from Helaman 13 (Samuel on the wall; the slippery treasures; happiness sought where it cannot be)
- person: `Samuel the Lamanite` (the outsider prophet on the wall тАФ cast out, sent back, prophesies destruction + the signs of Christ)
- doctrine: `happiness-sought-in-iniquity-is-structurally-impossible` (13:38 тАФ contrary to the nature of righteousness; Alma 41:10 as ontology) ┬╖ `the-curse-is-the-heart-set-on-riches-not-the-riches` (13:21-22) ┬╖ `the-righteous-are-what-hold-back-destruction` (13:12-14) ┬╖ `procrastinating-salvation-until-everlastingly-too-late` (13:38) ┬╖ theme: `the-slippery-treasures` (13:31-37 тАФ fulfilled Mormon 1:18) ┬╖ `the-outsider-prophet-God-sends-the-messenger-you'd-reject` (13:2-4) ┬╖ `tomb-builders-honor-dead-prophets-kill-living-ones` (13:24-26) ┬╖ `the-flatterer-is-welcomed-the-truth-teller-killed` (13:27-28)

### from Helaman 14 (the dated signs; the two deaths; ye are free)
- person: `Samuel the Lamanite` (the dated signs of Christ's birth + death; the two redemptions; agency)
- doctrine: `the-two-deaths-and-the-two-tiered-redemption` (14:16-18 тАФ first death universal/free, second death conditional) ┬╖ `the-resurrection-redeems-all-mankind-unconditionally` (14:16-17) ┬╖ `ye-are-free-God-hath-made-you-free` (14:30-31 тАФ the agency climax) ┬╖ `agency-requires-knowledge-freedom-and-real-consequence` (14:30-31) ┬╖ `whosoever-perisheth-perisheth-unto-himself` (14:30) ┬╖ theme: `the-dated-falsifiable-signs-leave-no-cause-for-unbelief` (14:2-28, fulfilled 3 Ne 1+8) ┬╖ `remember-that-you-are-free` (14:30 тАФ the Helaman refrain on agency)

### from Helaman 15 (Samuel's close: chastening as love; the steadfast converts)
- person: `Samuel the Lamanite` (closes his prophecy)
- doctrine: `chastening-is-the-proof-of-love-not-its-absence` (15:3 тАФ "chastened them because he loveth them"; the affliction-arc capstone) ┬╖ `the-converts-from-darkness-hold-the-light-more-firmly-than-the-born-in` (15:5-10) ┬╖ `the-curse-tracks-deeds-rooted-in-tradition-not-blood` (15:4 тАФ with-Michael 2 Ne 5 thread) ┬╖ `the-latter-day-mercy-and-restoration-of-the-Lamanite-remnant` (15:11-13) ┬╖ `less-light-more-faith-the-privileged-convicted-by-the-deprived` (15:14-15, Matt 11:21) ┬╖ theme: `love-fully-exercised-can-still-end-in-the-beloved's-destruction` (15:3, 16-17) ┬╖ `the-two-destinies-sealed` (15:16-17 тАФ fulfilled)

### from Helaman 16 (the close; the miracle reassigned to the devil)
- person: `Samuel the Lamanite` (protected on the wall; flees, never heard of again) ┬╖ `Nephi (son of Helaman)` (baptizing, working miracles before Christ's coming)
- doctrine: `when-the-miracle-cannot-be-denied-the-hardened-heart-reassigns-its-source` (16:6 тАФ "he hath a devil") ┬╖ `the-purpose-of-prophecy-is-remembrance-that-becomes-future-faith` (16:4-5) ┬╖ theme: `the-modern-rationalizations-against-prophecy` (16:16-21) ┬╖ `religion-as-a-control-mechanism-the-clerical-control-suspicion` (16:20-21) ┬╖ `depending-on-one's-own-wisdom-is-the-root-of-the-rationalizing` (16:15, Isa 5:21) ┬╖ `opposition-intensifies-as-the-evidence-intensifies` (16:13-23)

## тАФ THE BOOK OF 3 NEPHI (the signs fulfilled тЖТ the great destruction тЖТ CHRIST DESCENDS тЖТ the Sermon at Bountiful тЖТ the Nephite Zion) тАФ

### from 3 Nephi 1 (the sign of Christ's birth; the last-hour deliverance)
- person: `Nephi (son of Nephi, son of Helaman)` (keeps the records; prays all day; receives the voice) ┬╖ `Nephi (son of Helaman)` (departs, "whither he went no man knoweth") ┬╖ `the premortal Christ` (speaks from heaven the night before His birth) ┬╖ `Lachoneus` (chief judge)
- doctrine: `the-God-who-speaks-from-heaven-is-the-God-about-to-be-born` (1:13-14) ┬╖ `Christ-is-both-Father-and-Son` (1:14 тАФ "the Father because of me, and of the Son because of my flesh"; Is-Jesus-Christ-God study) ┬╖ `the-law-of-Moses-not-abolished-before-Christ-fulfills-it` (1:24-25) ┬╖ theme: `faith-tested-to-the-death-deadline-and-the-last-hour-deliverance` (1:9-15) ┬╖ `the-sign-fulfilled-every-whit-prophecy-vindicated` (1:15-21) ┬╖ `the-persecutor's-plan-of-destruction-frustrated` (1:16) ┬╖ `Satan-works-to-make-people-disbelieve-what-they-saw` (1:22) ┬╖ `the-rising-generation-lost-to-flattery-righteousness-not-inherited` (1:29-30)

### from 3 Nephi 2 (the forgetting of the signs; the curse lifted on covenant)
- person: `Nephi (son of Nephi)` (keeper of records) ┬╖ `the converted Lamanites` (united, numbered + called Nephites, curse lifted)
- doctrine: `familiarity-dulls-the-miracle-the-three-stage-forgetting` (2:1 тАФ less astonished тЖТ hard/blind тЖТ disbelieve) ┬╖ `the-curse-is-lifted-on-covenant-affiliation` (2:14-16 тАФ with-Michael 2 Ne 5 thread; literal-skin residue for Michael) ┬╖ theme: `the-calendar-remembers-what-the-heart-forgets` (2:7-8 тАФ time reckoned from Christ) ┬╖ `the-dissolution-of-race-into-covenant` (2:11-16) ┬╖ `Christ-comes-to-a-people-who-forgot-the-sign` (2:19)

### from 3 Nephi 3 (Giddianhi's letter; Gidgiddoni's defensive war)
- person: `Giddianhi` (Gadianton chief; the inverted-conscience epistle) ┬╖ `Lachoneus` (just governor; refuses fear + negotiation) ┬╖ `Gidgiddoni` (the prophet-general)
- doctrine: `God-delivers-the-defender-not-the-aggressor` (3:20-21 тАФ even against evil men, no offensive war) ┬╖ `the-righteous-response-to-threat-is-prayer-plus-preparation-plus-repentance` (3:12-16) ┬╖ theme: `the-inverted-conscience-calling-evil-good` (3:9 тАФ "the works thereof I know to be good") ┬╖ `the-aggressor-reframes-himself-as-the-victim` (3:10-11) ┬╖ `the-prophet-general-military-command-joined-to-spiritual-gift` (3:18-19) ┬╖ `the-combination-recruits-as-brotherhood` (3:6-7)

### from 3 Nephi 4 (the great battle; the song of the delivered)
- person: `Gidgiddoni` (defensive strategy vindicated) ┬╖ `Giddianhi` (slain fleeing) ┬╖ `Zemnarihah` (the siege-layer; hanged, the tree felled)
- doctrine: `fear-of-God-displaces-fear-of-men-the-un-terrorizable-heart` (4:8-10) ┬╖ `in-the-strength-of-the-Lord-not-their-own` (4:10, 33 тАФ inverse of Hel 4:13) ┬╖ `the-delivered-give-all-the-glory-to-God-and-credit-repentance` (4:31-33) ┬╖ theme: `starve-the-parasite-deny-the-host` (4:1-6, 16-22) ┬╖ `provisioning-as-the-prudence-that-makes-deliverance-possible` (4:4, 18) ┬╖ `vigilance-not-victory-is-the-permanent-posture-against-the-combinations` (4:28-29)

### from 3 Nephi 5 (Mormon steps forward; the gathering of Israel)
- person: `Mormon` (the abridger steps forward by name; disciple of Christ) ┬╖ `Nephi (son of Nephi)` (whose record Mormon abridges)
- doctrine: `the-record-is-a-disciple's-testimony-for-a-salvific-purpose` (5:12-18) ┬╖ `the-combination-is-ended-by-the-dual-method-mercy-to-the-repentant-justice-to-the-unrepentant` (5:4-6 тАФ Hel 6:37 finally applied) ┬╖ `the-gathering-of-Israel-is-the-book's-purpose` (5:21-26 тАФ the remnant brought to Christ) ┬╖ `the-spiritual-gathering-precedes-the-geographic` (5:26) ┬╖ theme: `the-abridger-writes-toward-a-future-scattered-reader` (5:14-26)

### from 3 Nephi 6 (the tragic turn: inequality, class, the fall of the republic)
- person: `Lachoneus (the son)` (governor in the collapse year) ┬╖ `the inspired prophets` (testify of Christ, murdered) ┬╖ `the corrupt judges/lawyers/high priests` (murder the prophets, revive the combination)
- doctrine: `the-only-thing-that-can-stop-a-prospering-people-is-their-own-sin` (6:5) ┬╖ `inequality-of-wealth-and-learning-breaks-up-the-church` (6:12-14 тАФ the inverse of the 4 Ne Zion) ┬╖ `willful-rebellion-against-known-light-is-the-graver-sin` (6:18) ┬╖ theme: `the-same-railing-makes-some-rail-back-and-others-grow-penitent` (6:13) ┬╖ `the-establishment-is-angriest-at-the-prophets` (6:21-23) ┬╖ `the-combination's-endgame-is-to-overthrow-the-republic-and-install-a-king` (6:28-30)

### from 3 Nephi 7 (the nation fragments; Nephi's ministry in the anarchy)
- person: `Nephi (son of Nephi)` (ministers; angels daily; raises his brother from the dead) ┬╖ `Jacob` (anti-Christ king of the combination, flees north)
- doctrine: `society-fragments-into-tribalism-when-the-binding-loyalty-is-lost` (7:2-6) ┬╖ `the-relapse-is-worse-than-never-having-known-the-dog-to-its-vomit` (7:8) ┬╖ `order-without-righteousness-civil-peace-with-stoned-prophets` (7:14) ┬╖ `undeniable-power-provokes-anger-not-faith-in-the-hardened` (7:18-20) ┬╖ theme: `faith-so-great-that-angels-minister-daily` (7:15, 18) ┬╖ `the-gospel's-ordinances-hold-even-when-the-society-collapses` (7:24-25)

### from 3 Nephi 8 (the great destruction; three days of darkness)
- person: `Nephi (son of Nephi)` (the "just man" keeper; his miracles vouch for the record)
- doctrine: `the-record's-reliability-rests-on-the-moral-purity-of-its-keeper` (8:1) ┬╖ `power-in-Christ's-name-requires-purity` (8:1) ┬╖ `the-creation-convulses-at-the-death-of-its-Creator` (8:5-18) ┬╖ `when-the-Light-of-the-world-died-the-world-went-dark-enough-to-feel` (8:20-23) ┬╖ theme: `the-destruction-fulfills-Samuel's-sign-exactly` (8:5-23, Hel 14) ┬╖ `the-too-late-repentance-the-recognition-that-comes-when-it-can-no-longer-save` (8:24-25) ┬╖ `delayed-repentance-is-never-only-about-the-self` (8:25)

### from 3 Nephi 9 (the voice of Christ from the darkness)
- person: `Jesus Christ (the voice in the darkness)` (pronounces the wo, declares His divinity, gives the invitation + new covenant)
- doctrine: `the-same-voice-pronounces-the-wo-and-extends-the-arm-of-mercy` (9:2-14 тАФ mercy the final word) ┬╖ `Christ's-full-divinity-declared-in-his-own-voice` (9:15-18 тАФ Creator/eternal/one with the Father/light+life/Alpha+Omega; Is-Jesus-Christ-God study) ┬╖ `the-broken-heart-and-contrite-spirit-replace-animal-sacrifice` (9:19-20 тАФ the new covenant) ┬╖ `the-baptism-of-fire-can-come-unfelt` (9:20) ┬╖ `receiving-Christ-makes-one-a-son-of-God` (9:17) ┬╖ `come-as-a-little-child` (9:22) ┬╖ theme: `the-city-is-destroyed-when-there-are-none-righteous-left` (9:11, 13) ┬╖ `the-Creator-came-to-his-own-and-was-rejected-by-what-he-made` (9:15-16)

### from 3 Nephi 10 (the hen-gathering lament; the light returns)
- person: `Jesus Christ (the voice)` (the hen-lament; the promise to manifest His body)
- doctrine: `the-hen-gathering-her-chickens-the-tenderest-image-of-Christ` (10:4-6) ┬╖ `the-three-tenses-of-Christ's-gathering` (10:4-6 тАФ have/would have/will gather) ┬╖ `ye-would-not-the-willingness-of-Christ-defeated-only-by-the-human-refusal` (10:5) ┬╖ theme: `mourning-turned-into-joy-the-third-day-morning` (10:9-10) ┬╖ `the-spared-are-those-who-received-the-prophets` (10:12) ┬╖ `we-are-the-remnant-of-the-seed-of-Joseph` (10:16-17) ┬╖ `the-promise-of-the-descent` (10:18-19)

### from 3 Nephi 11 (CHRIST DESCENDS тАФ the heart of the book)
- person: `Jesus Christ (descended)` (the risen Lord in white; declares His Atonement; gives the doctrine) ┬╖ `the Father` (the voice: "my Beloved Son... hear ye him") ┬╖ `Nephi (son of Nephi)` (kisses His feet; given power to baptize)
- doctrine: `the-Father-always-points-to-the-Son-hear-ye-him` (11:7) ┬╖ `the-still-small-voice-understood-only-when-the-hearer-attunes` (11:3-6) ┬╖ `the-resurrected-Christ-keeps-the-wounds-the-marks-of-the-Atonement-are-eternal` (11:14-15) ┬╖ `Christ-meets-souls-one-by-one-not-as-a-mass` (11:15) ┬╖ `contention-is-of-the-devil-the-father-of-contention` (11:28-30) ┬╖ `the-doctrine-of-Christ-the-rock-believe-repent-be-baptized-become-as-a-child` (11:31-39) ┬╖ `declare-more-or-less-than-the-doctrine-and-it-comes-of-evil` (11:40) ┬╖ `the-Godhead-are-one` (11:27, 36 тАФ Is-Jesus-Christ-God study)

## тАФ THE SERMON AT THE TEMPLE (3 Nephi 12-14: the post-resurrection counterpart to the Sermon on the Mount, Matt 5-7, with Nephite variants) тАФ

### from 3 Nephi 12 (Sermon at the Temple I: Beatitudes, higher law, be perfect)
- person: `Jesus Christ` (delivers the Sermon) ┬╖ `the twelve Nephite disciples` (called, power to baptize)
- doctrine: `the-Beatitudes-are-wrapped-in-the-doctrine-of-Christ` (12:1-6) ┬╖ `more-blessed-are-they-who-believe-the-witnesses-words-without-seeing` (12:2 тАФ reaches the latter-day reader) ┬╖ `the-law-is-now-fulfilled-old-things-done-away-all-things-new` (12:18, 46-47) ┬╖ `the-higher-law-governs-the-heart-not-just-the-act` (12:21-44) ┬╖ `the-higher-law-on-anger-comes-right-after-contention-named-as-of-the-devil` (12:22 тАФ "without a cause" omitted) ┬╖ `be-perfect-even-as-I-the-resurrected-Christ-adds-himself-as-the-standard` (12:48, teleios) ┬╖ theme: `salt-and-light-as-gift-and-commission` (12:13-16)

### from 3 Nephi 13 (Sermon at the Temple II: secret worship, treasures, take-no-thought)
- person: `Jesus Christ` (the inward worship, the Lord's Prayer, the take-no-thought charge) ┬╖ `the twelve` (addressed directly in v25 as the called ministers)
- doctrine: `they-have-their-reward-the-human-applause-is-the-hypocrite's-full-wage` (13:2, 5, 16) ┬╖ `where-your-treasure-is-there-will-your-heart-be-the-heart-follows-the-treasure` (13:21) ┬╖ `the-single-eye-and-the-two-masters-undivided-devotion` (13:22-24) ┬╖ `take-no-thought-is-the-charge-to-the-called-twelve-not-blanket-counsel` (13:25-34 тАФ the Nephite interpretive key) ┬╖ `seek-ye-first-the-kingdom-and-all-these-things-shall-be-added` (13:33) ┬╖ `forgiveness-is-conditioned-on-our-forgiving` (13:14-15)

### from 3 Nephi 14 (Sermon at the Temple III, close: golden rule, fruits, "I never knew you", the rock)
- person: `Jesus Christ` (completes the Sermon)
- doctrine: `cast-the-beam-from-your-own-eye-first-then-help-your-brother` (14:1-5) ┬╖ `the-Father-gives-good-gifts-lesser-to-greater` (14:7-11) ┬╖ `the-golden-rule-is-the-law-and-the-prophets-stated-actively` (14:12) ┬╖ `the-strait-gate-the-narrow-way-the-few` (14:13-14) ┬╖ `by-their-fruits-ye-shall-know-them` (14:15-20) ┬╖ `I-never-knew-you-salvation-is-relational-not-the-works-resume` (14:21-23) ┬╖ `the-house-on-the-rock-is-hearing-AND-doing` (14:24-27 тАФ the storm beats both houses)

### from 3 Nephi 15 (the law fulfilled; "I am he that gave the law"; the other sheep)
- person: `Jesus Christ` (declares Himself the Lawgiver/Jehovah; reveals the other sheep) ┬╖ `the twelve` ("a light unto this people, a remnant of the house of Joseph")
- doctrine: `I-am-he-that-gave-the-law-Christ-is-Jehovah` (15:5 тАФ the God of Sinai is the risen Christ; Is-Jesus-Christ-God study) ┬╖ `the-law-of-Moses-ended-in-Christ-but-the-covenant-continues` (15:4-8) ┬╖ `I-am-the-law-the-law-replaced-by-a-Person-look-unto-me` (15:9) ┬╖ `other-sheep-one-fold-one-shepherd-the-flock-spans-the-earth` (15:17, 21) ┬╖ theme: `Christ-came-in-person-to-the-other-sheep-they-were-not-second-class` (15:24) ┬╖ `iniquity-shrinks-the-capacity-to-receive-truth` (15:18) ┬╖ `Israel-separated-because-of-iniquity-judgment-and-preservation-in-one-act` (15:19-20)

### from 3 Nephi 16 (the record to the Gentiles; the conditional fulness; Zion brought again)
- person: `Jesus Christ` (reveals the lost tribes; commands the record; warns the Gentiles; quotes Isaiah) ┬╖ `the lost tribes` (the other other sheep)
- doctrine: `the-record-made-for-the-Gentiles-to-reach-the-remnant` (16:4 тАФ the Book of Mormon's purpose/route) ┬╖ `the-gospel-comes-to-the-Gentiles-first-in-the-latter-days` (16:6-7, Rom 11) ┬╖ `the-fulness-can-be-taken-away-if-the-Gentiles-reject-it-in-pride` (16:10-15 тАФ a contemporary indictment) ┬╖ `the-repentant-Gentiles-are-numbered-among-Israel` (16:13) ┬╖ theme: `the-Gentile-reader-is-the-bridge-not-the-destination` (16:4) ┬╖ `contention-healed-in-Zion-the-watchmen-see-eye-to-eye` (16:18, Isa 52:8) ┬╖ `the-gathering-ends-in-a-song-not-a-judgment` (16:18-20, Isa 52:9-10)

### from 3 Nephi 17 (the tenderest chapter: compassion, the children, the angels of fire)
- person: `Jesus Christ` (compassion, healing, the unwritable prayer, weeping, blessing the children) ┬╖ `the little children` (blessed one by one, encircled with fire, ministered by angels тАФ the climax)
- doctrine: `compassion-changed-His-plan-He-stayed-for-a-weeping-people` (17:1-7) ┬╖ `my-bowels-are-filled-with-compassion-the-visceral-love-that-acts` (17:6-9) ┬╖ `Christ-paces-His-teaching-to-our-capacity` (17:2-3) ┬╖ `they-are-not-lost-unto-the-Father-nothing-is-lost-to-God` (17:4) ┬╖ `the-prayer-that-cannot-be-written-the-boundary-of-language` (17:14-17) ┬╖ theme: `Christ-wept-twice-from-fullness-not-grief` (17:21-22) ┬╖ `the-children-are-the-climax-angels-of-fire-for-the-least` (17:21-24) ┬╖ `the-tenderest-scene-is-also-the-most-carefully-witnessed` (17:25 тАФ 2,500)

### from 3 Nephi 18 (the sacrament instituted; watch and pray; the light to hold up)
- person: `Jesus Christ` (institutes the sacrament; gives the charges; confers the Holy Ghost; ascends) ┬╖ `the twelve disciples` (given power to give the Holy Ghost, touched one by one)
- doctrine: `the-sacrament-always-remember-me-and-ye-shall-have-my-Spirit` (18:7, 11) ┬╖ `watch-and-pray-always-Satan-desires-to-sift-you-as-wheat` (18:15-18) ┬╖ `pray-in-your-families` (18:21) ┬╖ `I-am-the-light-which-ye-shall-hold-up-the-borrowed-light` (18:24) ┬╖ `forbid-the-unworthy-from-the-sacrament-but-never-cast-out-the-person` (18:28-32) ┬╖ theme: `discipleship-is-a-continuous-posture-not-discrete-acts` (18:7-21 тАФ the recurring "always") ┬╖ `the-commandments-are-the-cure-for-contention` (18:34)

### from 3 Nephi 19 (the disciples filled with fire; the prayer to Jesus; made white as He is)
- person: `Jesus Christ` (the intercessory prayer; transfigures the disciples) ┬╖ `the twelve disciples` (named; baptized; filled with the Holy Ghost + fire; made white as Christ)
- doctrine: `the-disciples-prayed-to-Jesus-as-their-Lord-and-their-God` (19:18, 22 тАФ worship of Christ; Is-Jesus-Christ-God study) ┬╖ `the-unity-prayer-believers-drawn-into-the-oneness-of-Father-and-Son` (19:23, 29) ┬╖ `purified-by-faith-Christ-glorified-in-the-believer` (19:28-29) ┬╖ `the-prayer-beyond-words-understood-in-the-open-heart` (19:32-34) ┬╖ `faith-unlocks-miracles-unbelief-constrains-even-Christ` (19:35) ┬╖ `Spirit-prompted-prayer-it-was-given-them-what-to-pray` (19:24) ┬╖ theme: `the-disciples-made-white-as-Christ-transfiguration-glory-not-race` (19:25, 30)

### from 3 Nephi 20 (the miraculous sacrament; the prophet like Moses; the gathering + Isaiah 52)
- person: `Jesus Christ` (provides the sacrament miraculously; the prophet like Moses; quotes Isaiah 52)
- doctrine: `the-miraculous-sacrament-the-bread-of-life-that-fills-the-soul-forever` (20:3-9, John 6) ┬╖ `the-Father-and-I-are-one-appended-to-Isaiah` (20:35 тАФ Is-Jesus-Christ-God study) ┬╖ `Christ-is-the-prophet-like-unto-Moses` (20:23, Deut 18) ┬╖ `the-blessing-of-Abraham's-seed-is-being-turned-from-iniquity` (20:25-27) ┬╖ `Israel-blessed-first-to-carry-the-blessing-to-all-kindreds` (20:26-27) ┬╖ theme: `the-remnant-as-a-lion-and-the-New-Jerusalem` (20:16-22, Micah 5) ┬╖ `the-redemption-of-Zion-the-beautiful-feet-awake-be-clean` (20:32-45, Isa 52)

### from 3 Nephi 21 (the sign of the gathering: the Book of Mormon; the New Jerusalem)
- person: `Jesus Christ` (gives the sign; prophesies the servant, the New Jerusalem) ┬╖ `the marred servant` (brings forth the book, preserved in the Lord's hand)
- doctrine: `the-Book-of-Mormon's-coming-forth-is-the-sign-the-gathering-has-begun` (21:1-7 тАФ the reader is inside the sign) ┬╖ `a-free-nation-established-providentially-so-the-book-could-come-forth` (21:4) ┬╖ `the-marred-but-preserved-servant-Gods-wisdom-greater-than-the-devils-cunning` (21:10) ┬╖ `the-two-Gentile-destinies-cut-off-or-numbered-among-Jacob` (21:14-22) ┬╖ theme: `the-repentant-Gentiles-become-co-builders-of-the-New-Jerusalem` (21:23-25) ┬╖ `the-gathering-of-all-the-dispersed-not-in-haste-God-before-and-behind` (21:26-29, Isa 52:12)

### from 3 Nephi 22 (Isaiah 54: the forsaken-then-gathered wife)
- person: `Jesus Christ` (quotes Isaiah 54 to comfort the Nephites about the gathering)
- doctrine: `for-a-small-moment-forsaken-with-everlasting-kindness-gathered-the-asymmetry` (22:7-8) ┬╖ `the-covenant-of-peace-is-more-permanent-than-the-mountains` (22:10) ┬╖ `God-is-Israel's-husband-the-covenant-as-marriage` (22:5-6) ┬╖ `all-thy-children-shall-be-taught-of-the-Lord` (22:13, new covenant) ┬╖ `no-weapon-formed-against-thee-shall-prosper-righteousness-of-me` (22:17) ┬╖ theme: `the-barren-woman-who-sings-the-desolate-made-most-fruitful` (22:1-3) ┬╖ `hope-enlarges-the-tent-before-the-children-come` (22:2-3)

### from 3 Nephi 23 (great are the words of Isaiah; the record audited)
- person: `Jesus Christ` (commands the search of Isaiah; audits the record; expounds the scriptures) ┬╖ `Nephi (son of Nephi)` (brings the record; remembers the omission; writes the correction)
- doctrine: `great-are-the-words-of-Isaiah-search-diligently` (23:1-3) ┬╖ `Christ-audits-the-record-for-completeness-and-accuracy` (23:6-13 тАФ resonant with read-before-quoting) ┬╖ `the-record-must-preserve-fulfillment-not-just-prophecy` (23:9-13) ┬╖ `Christ-expounds-the-scriptures-in-one-then-the-disciples-teach` (23:14) ┬╖ theme: `the-right-response-to-a-found-gap-is-acknowledge-and-correct` (23:11-13)

### from 3 Nephi 24 (Malachi 3 тАФ messenger, refiner's fire, "prove me," book of remembrance)
- person: `Jesus Christ (the messenger of the covenant)` (dictates Malachi; came suddenly to the temple, will come again) ┬╖ `Heavenly Father` ("the words which the Father had given unto Malachi") ┬╖ `Malachi` (the prophet c. 430 BC the Nephites never had)
- doctrine: `Christ-supplies-the-prophecy-the-Nephites-never-had` (24:1 тАФ completes the record forward as ch 23 completed it backward) ┬╖ `Christ-the-messenger-of-the-covenant-came-suddenly-to-his-temple` (24:1 тАФ dramatic irony + dual horizon) ┬╖ `the-refiners-fire-purifies-not-only-punishes` (24:2-3) ┬╖ `God-is-a-swift-witness-against-oppression-of-the-vulnerable` (24:5) ┬╖ `God-changes-not-therefore-Jacob-is-not-consumed` (24:6 тАФ immutability as mercy) ┬╖ `prove-me-now-herewith-the-one-invited-test-tithing` (24:8-12) ┬╖ `God-keeps-a-book-of-remembrance-of-those-who-fear-him` (24:16-18 тАФ heavenly record mirrors ch 23's earthly audit) ┬╖ theme: `they-that-feared-the-Lord-spake-often-one-to-another` (24:16)

### from 3 Nephi 25 (Malachi 4 тАФ the day that burns and heals; Elijah)
- person: `Jesus Christ (the Son of Righteousness)` (reads the prophecy that names Himself; the risen Son with healing in His wings) ┬╖ `Elijah` (sent before the great and dreadful day to turn hearts) ┬╖ `Moses` (the law given at Horeb, remembered though fulfilled)
- doctrine: `one-day-two-destinies-the-same-fire-burns-and-heals` (25:1-2) ┬╖ `the-Son-of-Righteousness-arises-with-healing-in-his-wings` (25:2 тАФ KJV "Sun"тЖТ"Son" variant) ┬╖ `remember-the-law-of-Moses-fulfilled-but-not-despised` (25:4) ┬╖ `Elijah-turns-the-hearts-of-the-generations-lest-the-earth-be-cursed` (25:5-6 тАФ sealing power) ┬╖ image: `the-faithful-grow-up-as-calves-released-from-the-stall` (25:2-3) ┬╖ theme: `the-last-word-of-the-prophets-is-family-not-wrath` (25:6)

### from 3 Nephi 26 (the lesser part to try faith; babes utter marvelous things; church established)
- person: `Jesus Christ (who was before the world began)` (expounds all things; looses the children's tongues) ┬╖ `Mormon` (writes only the lesser part, forbidden the greater) ┬╖ `the children/babes of the multitude` (revelators of things greater than the adults received)
- doctrine: `Christ-expounds-all-things-from-the-beginning-to-the-last-day` (26:1-5) ┬╖ `the-record-is-given-for-future-generations-by-the-Fathers-command` (26:2) ┬╖ `the-lesser-part-is-given-first-to-try-faith-belief-unlocks-the-greater` (26:6-11 тАФ the load-bearing doctrine; BoM = entrance exam for the sealed portion) ┬╖ `out-of-the-mouth-of-babes-the-children-become-revelators` (26:14, 16) ┬╖ `the-church-of-Christ-established-baptism-Holy-Ghost-all-things-common` (26:17-21 тАФ seed of 4 Nephi's Zion) ┬╖ theme: `unspeakable-things-not-lawful-to-be-written` (26:18)

### from 3 Nephi 27 (the name + the gospel defined; "even as I am")
- person: `Jesus Christ` (names the church, defines His gospel, sets "even as I am," rejoices and sorrows) ┬╖ `the twelve Nephite disciples` (united in fasting; commanded to write + be judges; asked "what manner of men ought ye to be?")
- doctrine: `the-church-must-bear-Christs-name-AND-be-built-on-his-gospel` (27:5-12 тАФ two requirements) ┬╖ `the-gospel-defined-by-Christ-himself` (27:13-21 тАФ fullest definition in scripture) ┬╖ `what-manner-of-men-ought-ye-to-be-even-as-I-am` (27:27 тАФ becoming like Christ) ┬╖ `out-of-the-books-shall-the-world-be-judged` (27:23-26 тАФ record's ultimate function) ┬╖ image: `washed-their-garments-in-my-blood` (27:19) ┬╖ theme: `Christ-has-fulness-of-joy-and-real-sorrow-at-once` (27:30-32) ┬╖ `enter-at-the-strait-gate-while-it-is-day` (27:33)

### from 3 Nephi 28 (the heart's desire; the three Nephites; translation)
- person: `Jesus Christ` (asks each disciple's desire; grants each according to his heart) ┬╖ `the nine disciples` (desire rest, granted at 72) ┬╖ `the three Nephites` (desire to tarry and bring souls; translated) ┬╖ `John the Beloved` (whose tarrying desire the three shared) ┬╖ `Mormon` (writes "I know not," inquires, corrects the record openly)
- doctrine: `the-question-of-the-hearts-desire-reveals-the-soul` (28:1-9) ┬╖ `the-more-blessed-desire-is-to-keep-bringing-souls-not-to-rest-sooner` (28:7-9) ┬╖ `the-chain-of-oneness-disciple-as-Christ-Christ-as-Father-Father-and-Son-one` (28:10-11 тАФ major is-jesus-christ-god datapoint) ┬╖ `transfiguration-is-the-enabling-condition-of-beholding-God` (28:15) ┬╖ `the-doctrine-of-translation-sanctified-in-the-flesh-but-not-yet-resurrected` (28:38-40) ┬╖ theme: `Mormon-models-the-honest-record-I-know-not-then-I-have-inquired` (28:17, 36-37) ┬╖ `the-OT-deliverance-types-multiplied-in-the-three-Nephites` (28:19-22)

### from 3 Nephi 29 (Mormon's direct address to the latter-day reader)
- person: `Mormon` (speaks in the second person to the latter-day Gentile reader of his finished book) ┬╖ `the latter-day Gentile reader` (warned how to respond to the record) ┬╖ `the house of Israel / the Jews` (the covenant people not cast off)
- doctrine: `the-coming-forth-of-the-record-is-the-sign-the-covenant-is-fulfilling` (29:1-3) ┬╖ `wo-to-cessationism-God-who-changes-not-still-works-by-revelation-and-gifts` (29:5-6) ┬╖ `denying-miracles-to-get-gain-is-priestcraft-likened-to-the-son-of-perdition` (29:7) ┬╖ `do-not-mock-the-Jews-or-Israel-the-covenant-stands` (29:8 тАФ prescient) ┬╖ `no-one-can-turn-the-Lords-right-hand-the-covenant-is-irreversible` (29:9) ┬╖ theme: `the-record-proves-God-has-not-stopped-acting-speaking-or-covenant-keeping` (29:1-9)

### from 3 Nephi 30 (the closing invitation)
- person: `Jesus Christ (the Son of the living God)` (issues the closing invitation in His own voice through Mormon) ┬╖ `the latter-day Gentiles` (commanded to turn, come, be baptized, be numbered with Israel)
- doctrine: `the-last-word-of-3-Nephi-is-invitation-not-condemnation` (30:1-2) ┬╖ `the-Gentile-who-comes-to-Christ-is-numbered-with-Israel` (30:2 тАФ the grafting-in) ┬╖ `the-warning-and-the-invitation-are-the-same-covenant` (29:8 + 30:2) ┬╖ theme: `the-book-opens-a-door-and-leaves-it-open-come-unto-me` (30:1-2)

## тАФ END OF 3 NEPHI (30/30) ┬╖ 4 NEPHI BEGINS тАФ

### from 4 Nephi 1 (the rise and fall of Zion in one chapter)
- person: `Nephi (son of Nephi), Amos, Amos, Ammaron` (the record-keeper line across the four-Nephi span; Ammaron hides the records) ┬╖ `the three Nephite disciples` (tarry; persecuted, delivered)
- doctrine: `Zion-was-actually-achieved-the-happiest-people-who-ever-lived` (1:1-18) ┬╖ `Zion-is-rooted-in-the-love-of-God-in-the-heart-not-in-enforced-economics` (1:15) ┬╖ `in-Zion-there-are-no-ites-all-are-one-the-children-of-Christ` (1:17) ┬╖ `the-ites-track-belief-not-blood-they-vanish-and-return-with-faith` (1:17 + 1:38 тАФ 2 Ne 5:21 bookends) ┬╖ `Zion-falls-through-pride-entering-by-costly-apparel` (1:24-26) ┬╖ `wilful-rebellion-against-known-gospel-is-worse-than-dwindling` (1:38-39) ┬╖ theme: `the-people-of-Jesus-did-not-smite-again` (1:34) ┬╖ `the-sacred-record-preserved-through-apostasy-for-the-latter-day-remnant` (1:48-49)

## тАФ END OF 4 NEPHI ┬╖ THE BOOK OF MORMON тАФ

### from Mormon 1 (the boy entrusted; the gifts withdrawn; the preacher forbidden)
- person: `Mormon` (the sober, observant child commissioned with the record; visited by the Lord at 15; forbidden to preach) ┬╖ `Ammaron` (entrusts the ten-year-old with the record's location and charge) ┬╖ `the three Nephites (beloved disciples)` (taken away as wickedness prevails)
- doctrine: `the-record-passes-to-character-sober-and-quick-to-observe` (1:2-5) ┬╖ `the-commission-of-the-witness-observe-remember-record` (1:3-4) ┬╖ `the-gifts-cease-through-the-peoples-unbelief-not-Gods-change` (1:13-14 тАФ inverse of 3 Ne 29 cessationism) ┬╖ `the-individual-of-a-sober-mind-is-visited-even-in-a-faithless-age` (1:15) ┬╖ `the-willing-preacher-forbidden-the-word-withdrawn-from-wilful-rebellion` (1:16-17) ┬╖ theme: `the-collapse-fulfills-the-prophets-Abinadi-and-Samuel-vindicated` (1:18-19)

### from Mormon 2 (the boy general; the sorrowing of the damned; the day of grace passed)
- person: `Mormon` (general at 16; rejoices then grieves over the false repentance; takes the plates; lifelong sorrow + hope) ┬╖ `king Aaron` (Lamanite king Mormon defeats)
- doctrine: `godly-sorrow-vs-the-sorrowing-of-the-damned` (2:12-13) ┬╖ `the-tell-is-the-direction-of-the-turn-toward-Christ-or-cursing-God` (2:14) ┬╖ `the-day-of-grace-can-pass-for-a-people-who-wilfully-harden` (2:15) ┬╖ `the-most-frightening-judgment-is-being-left-to-ourselves` (2:26 тАФ covenant's reversal) ┬╖ theme: `the-prophets-lifelong-grief-and-unshaken-hope` (2:18-19) ┬╖ `the-boy-trusted-with-their-bodies-refused-with-their-souls` (2:1-2)

### from Mormon 3 (the vengeance-oath; Mormon refuses to lead; the turn to the reader)
- person: `Mormon` (cries repentance again; refuses to lead the vengeance-war; "an idle witness"; addresses the reader) ┬╖ `Jesus Christ (the very Christ and the very God)` (the divinity the record exists to witness)
- doctrine: `the-Lord-renews-the-offer-of-mercy-even-past-the-day-of-grace` (3:2) ┬╖ `ingratitude-is-failing-to-perceive-that-it-was-the-Lord-who-spared-you` (3:3) ┬╖ `boasting-in-own-strength-and-the-vengeance-oath-cross-from-defensive-to-offensive-war` (3:9-10) ┬╖ `Mormon-refuses-to-lead-conscientious-objection-love-without-faith` (3:11-12) ┬╖ `vengeance-is-mine-usurping-Gods-vengeance-is-the-final-sin` (3:14-15) ┬╖ `the-idle-witness-when-you-cannot-fix-it-witness-truthfully` (3:16) ┬╖ `the-Book-of-Mormon-is-the-other-witness-that-Jesus-is-the-very-God` (3:21 тАФ is-jesus-christ-god datapoint) ┬╖ theme: `the-idle-witness-is-the-most-active-missionary-reaching-past-his-own-people-to-the-reader` (3:17-22)

### from Mormon 4 (the offensive war turns; by the wicked are the wicked punished)
- person: `Mormon` (narrates the collapse; names the theology of judgment; secures the full record from Shim)
- doctrine: `the-offensive-war-strips-the-defense-the-aggression-itself-makes-them-vulnerable` (4:4) ┬╖ `it-is-by-the-wicked-that-the-wicked-are-punished` (4:5) ┬╖ `the-final-hardening-is-delighting-in-the-shedding-of-blood` (4:11-12 тАФ Noah-level, worst in all Israel) ┬╖ theme: `the-sacrifice-of-innocents-and-the-cycle-of-rage-not-repentance` (4:14-15, 21) ┬╖ `the-record-walks-out-of-the-collapse-alive` (4:23) ┬╖ image: `swept-off-even-as-a-dew-before-the-sun` (4:18)

### from Mormon 5 (leading without hope; why the record comes forth; the covenant remembered)
- person: `Mormon` (repents of his oath, leads "without hope"; explains the record's purpose; warns the Gentiles) ┬╖ `Jesus Christ (the Christ, the Son of the living God)` (the divinity the record exists to persuade men of)
- doctrine: `leading-without-hope-fidelity-without-expectation-of-victory` (5:1-2) ┬╖ `the-record-comes-forth-to-persuade-that-Jesus-is-the-Christ-and-to-gather-Israel` (5:14 тАФ is-jesus-christ-god datapoint) ┬╖ `the-mercy-in-the-editing-truth-told-but-the-full-horror-spared` (5:8-9) ┬╖ `the-Spirit-ceasing-to-strive-leaves-a-people-as-chaff-and-a-rudderless-ship` (5:16-18) ┬╖ `the-covenant-outlasts-the-fall-the-Lord-remembers-after-the-scattering` (5:19-20) ┬╖ `the-prayers-of-the-righteous-are-banked-and-answered-generations-later` (5:21) ┬╖ **bin4**: `dark-filthy-loathsome-because-of-unbelief-and-idolatry` (5:15 тАФ FLAGGED for Michael, NOT resolved) ┬╖ theme: `the-Gentiles-are-warned-they-too-are-in-the-hands-of-God` (5:22-24)

### from Mormon 6 (Cumorah: the record hidden, the nation fallen, the lament)
- person: `Mormon` (hides the records in Cumorah, gives the abridgment to Moroni; falls wounded; laments) ┬╖ `Moroni` (Mormon's son; survives Cumorah; receives the few plates to finish the record) ┬╖ `the named captains (Gidgiddonah, Lamah, Gilgal, Limhah, Jeneum...)` (fell, each with his ten thousand)
- doctrine: `the-record-secured-at-the-moment-of-national-death-the-priority-that-outlasts-everything` (6:6) ┬╖ `the-tragedy-was-avoidable-Jesus-stood-with-open-arms` (6:17-18) ┬╖ `the-lament-turns-to-the-resurrection-and-the-judgment` (6:21) ┬╖ `committing-the-dead-to-God-who-knows-their-state-and-acts-in-justice-and-mercy` (6:22) ┬╖ theme: `the-roll-call-of-the-ten-thousands-refuses-to-let-the-dead-be-a-statistic` (6:11-15) ┬╖ `the-dead-grieved-as-families-not-combatants` (6:19-20)

### from Mormon 7 (the dying prophet's farewell to the Lamanite remnant)
- person: `Mormon` (closes his record blessing the latter-day Lamanite remnant; no curse, only invitation) ┬╖ `the latter-day Lamanite remnant` (descendants of his enemies, addressed as Israel, invited to Christ) ┬╖ `Jesus Christ (the Son of God; one God with Father + Holy Ghost)` (the center of the compressed gospel)
- doctrine: `the-dying-prophets-last-words-bless-the-descendants-of-his-enemies` (7:1-2) ┬╖ `identity-comes-first-know-ye-that-ye-are-of-the-house-of-Israel` (7:2, 10) ┬╖ `lay-down-your-weapons-delight-no-more-in-the-shedding-of-blood` (7:4) ┬╖ `the-compressed-gospel-Son-of-God-slain-risen-victor-over-the-grave` (7:5-7) ┬╖ `the-Father-Son-and-Holy-Ghost-are-one-God` (7:7 тАФ is-jesus-christ-god datapoint) ┬╖ `the-Bible-and-the-Book-of-Mormon-are-mutual-witnesses` (7:8-9) ┬╖ theme: `it-shall-be-well-with-you-the-last-word-is-blessing-not-lament` (7:10)

### from Mormon 8 (Moroni alone; the record from the dust; he sees our day)
- person: `Moroni` (the last Nephite; finishes the record alone; is shown the latter-day reader; warns us) ┬╖ `Jesus Christ` (who showed Moroni the latter-day reader)
- doctrine: `Moroni-alone-faithfulness-when-every-external-reason-for-hope-is-gone` (8:1-5) ┬╖ `the-record-is-imperfect-but-true-condemn-it-not-the-faults-are-mens` (8:12, 17) ┬╖ `the-plates-are-worthless-the-record-is-priceless-not-for-gain` (8:14-16) ┬╖ `the-eternal-purposes-of-the-Lord-roll-on-the-work-cannot-be-stopped` (8:21-22) ┬╖ `the-record-speaks-from-the-dust-as-if-one-should-speak-from-the-dead` (8:23-26) ┬╖ `Moroni-was-shown-our-day-and-addresses-us-directly` (8:34-35 тАФ "Jesus Christ hath shown you unto me") ┬╖ `the-indictment-of-our-day-is-pride-and-very-fine-apparel` (8:36) ┬╖ `the-measuring-line-loving-money-and-adornment-more-than-the-poor` (8:37, 39)

### from Mormon 9 (the God of miracles who changes not; Moroni's farewell)
- person: `Moroni` (appeals to the unbeliever; argues for a God of miracles; gives the farewell of his father's book) ┬╖ `God (the same yesterday, today, and forever)` (the immutable God whose unchangingness proves He still works miracles)
- doctrine: `hell-is-the-misery-of-the-unclean-soul-in-the-presence-of-holiness` (9:3-5) ┬╖ `a-god-who-changes-is-no-God-immutability-is-deity` (9:9-10) ┬╖ `God-still-works-miracles-because-He-changes-not` (9:15-19 тАФ climax of the anti-cessationism argument) ┬╖ `miracles-cease-only-because-people-dwindle-in-unbelief` (9:20) ┬╖ `signs-follow-those-who-believe-doubting-nothing` (9:21-25) ┬╖ `the-fixity-of-character-at-judgment-filthy-still-righteous-still` (9:14) ┬╖ `condemn-not-the-records-imperfections-give-thanks-and-be-wiser` (9:31-34) ┬╖ theme: `the-watchmans-discharge-rid-our-garments-of-the-blood-of-our-brethren` (9:35) ┬╖ `the-book-closes-on-the-covenant-not-the-destruction` (9:36-37)

## тАФ END OF MORMON (9/9) ┬╖ THE BOOK OF ETHER BEGINS тАФ

### from Ether 1 (the Jaredite record begins; the brother of Jared; the choice land)
- person: `Moroni` (abridges the Jaredite record from the 24 plates) ┬╖ `Ether` (the last Jaredite prophet, whose record Moroni abridges) ┬╖ `the brother of Jared` ("a large and mighty man, highly favored of the Lord"; the intercessor at the tower) ┬╖ `Jared` (prompts his brother to cry unto the Lord; reaches in faith toward the choice land)
- doctrine: `Ether-is-a-second-independent-witness-the-same-covenant-the-same-rise-and-fall` (1:1-5, 42) ┬╖ `the-record-nested-three-deep-Moroni-abridging-Ether-recording-the-Jaredites` (1:1-6) ┬╖ `the-brother-of-Jared-the-intercessor-prayer-that-widens-to-include-others` (1:34-37) ┬╖ `the-Lord-had-compassion-the-God-of-justice-is-also-the-God-of-compassion` (1:35, 37, 40) ┬╖ `faith-reaches-past-the-crisis-toward-the-promise-and-binds-itself-in-advance` (1:38-43) ┬╖ theme: `the-choice-land-opened-because-this-long-time-ye-have-cried-unto-me` (1:42-43)

### from Ether 2 (the choice-land decree; the chastening; "what will ye that I should do?")
- person: `the brother of Jared` (led to the choice land; chastened for neglecting prayer; asked to propose the solution) ┬╖ `Jesus Christ (the God of the land)` (the God who swore the decree of the land)
- doctrine: `the-choice-land-decree-serve-God-or-be-swept-off` (2:7-10) ┬╖ `the-sweeping-off-comes-only-when-iniquity-is-full-the-long-suffering-in-the-decree` (2:9-10) ┬╖ `national-freedom-is-conditioned-on-serving-the-God-of-the-land-who-is-Jesus-Christ` (2:11-12 тАФ is-jesus-christ-god datapoint) ┬╖ `even-the-favored-neglect-prayer-the-three-hour-chastening` (2:14) ┬╖ `the-Spirit-will-not-always-strive-with-man` (2:15) ┬╖ `God-answers-prayer-with-a-question-what-will-ye-that-I-should-do` (2:18-25)

### from Ether 3 (the brother of Jared within the veil; "I am Jesus Christ")
- person: `the brother of Jared` (molds the 16 stones; sees the finger then the whole body of the premortal Christ; faith perfected into knowledge) ┬╖ `Jesus Christ (the premortal Lord; the Father and the Son)` (reveals Himself in His spirit body; "I am Jesus Christ") ┬╖ `Moroni` (narrating; "that this man might know that he was God")
- doctrine: `faith-and-works-meet-man-does-his-part-God-does-what-only-God-can` (3:1-5) ┬╖ `humility-about-self-and-boldness-about-God-are-the-two-halves-of-faith` (3:2-5) ┬╖ **`I-am-Jesus-Christ-I-am-the-Father-and-the-Son-the-premortal-Christs-self-declaration`** (3:14 тАФ FOUNDATIONAL is-jesus-christ-god datapoint) ┬╖ `the-imago-Dei-man-created-after-the-body-of-Gods-spirit` (3:15-16) ┬╖ `that-this-man-might-know-that-he-was-God` (3:18 тАФ is-jesus-christ-god) ┬╖ `faith-perfected-becomes-knowledge-and-cannot-be-kept-from-within-the-veil` (3:19-20) ┬╖ `faith-that-God-CAN-show-all-things-unlocks-all-things` (3:25-26) ┬╖ theme: `the-sealed-record-and-the-interpreters` (3:21-28)

### from Ether 4 (the greater things wait on the greater faith; "rend that veil of unbelief")
- person: `Moroni` (has sealed the brother of Jared's full vision with the interpreters) ┬╖ `Jesus Christ (the Son of God; the Father of heaven and earth; the light, the life, the truth)` (calls men to rend the veil of unbelief)
- doctrine: `the-greater-things-wait-on-the-greater-faith-faith-like-the-brother-of-Jared` (4:6-7) ┬╖ `Jesus-Christ-the-Son-of-God-the-Father-of-heaven-and-earth-I-am-the-light-and-the-life-and-the-truth` (4:7, 12 тАФ is-jesus-christ-god) ┬╖ `whatsoever-persuades-men-to-do-good-is-of-Christ-the-Spirit-confirms-truth-by-persuading-to-good` (4:11-12) ┬╖ `rend-that-veil-of-unbelief-the-veil-is-ours-not-Gods` (4:13-15) ┬╖ `the-veil-is-rent-by-a-broken-heart-and-a-contrite-spirit` (4:15) ┬╖ theme: `the-records-coming-forth-is-the-sign-the-work-of-the-Father-has-commenced` (4:17)

### from Ether 5 (Moroni's word to the translator; the three witnesses)
- person: `Moroni` (speaks directly to the future translator; prophesies the witnesses; stakes his authority on the judgment) ┬╖ `the future translator (Joseph Smith)` (addressed by task; forbidden the sealed portion) ┬╖ `the Three Witnesses` (to be shown the plates by the power of God)
- doctrine: `Moroni-addresses-the-translator-directly-the-writers-were-shown-their-readers` (5:1) ┬╖ `the-law-of-witnesses-three-men-plus-the-fourfold-divine-testimony` (5:2-4 тАФ Father, Son, Holy Ghost bear record) ┬╖ `the-testimony-stands-against-the-world-at-the-last-day-but-the-door-is-open` (5:4-5) ┬╖ `Moroni-stakes-his-authority-on-meeting-the-reader-at-the-judgment` (5:6)

### from Ether 6 (the crossing; praise in the storm; "this thing leadeth into captivity")
- person: `the brother of Jared` (places the stones; praises through the storm; warns against a king; dies) ┬╖ `Jared` (overrules the warning: "suffer them that they may have a king") ┬╖ `Orihah` (the righteous first Jaredite king) ┬╖ `Pagag` (firstborn who refuses the kingship)
- doctrine: `the-storm-that-buries-them-is-the-wind-that-drives-them-home` (6:5-8) ┬╖ `praise-all-the-day-long-in-the-storm-gratitude-in-the-tempest` (6:9-10) ┬╖ `the-light-God-gives-holds-even-under-the-waves` (6:10) ┬╖ `surely-this-thing-leadeth-into-captivity-the-anti-monarchy-warning` (6:22-24) ┬╖ `kingship-cannot-be-forced-constrain-no-man-to-be-your-king` (6:25-27) ┬╖ theme: `the-journey-through-the-storm-ends-in-worship-and-tears-of-joy` (6:11-12) ┬╖ `a-good-first-king-delays-but-does-not-remove-the-structural-danger` (6:28-30)
