- `doctrine:the-record-passes-to-character-sober-and-quick-to-observe` тАФ[Ammaron looks at a ten-year-old and sees the two qualities a record-keeper needs: "I perceive that thou art a sober child, and art quick to observe" тАФ serious/trustworthy + perceptive/attentive, the qualities of a true witness and faithful historian, visible in a child; chosen not for lineage or office or learning but for CHARACTER, the kind of person he already was at ten; the Lord's record passed to the man who as a boy was sober and saw clearly]тЖТ 1:2-5 (4 Ne 1:48-49; Mosiah 1:3-5; 1 Sam 16:7; D&C 11:21)
- `doctrine:the-commission-of-the-witness-observe-remember-record` тАФ["remember the things that ye have observed concerning this people... engrave on the plates of Nephi all the things that ye have observed"; a fourteen-year gap built in (told at 10, come at 24) тАФ the boy carries the charge while observing all the while; the whole intervening time is the assignment: watch your people with the eyes of one who will have to write them down truthfully; a person entrusted in advance with bearing witness lives and attends differently тАФ Mormon's whole youth a long act of observation under commission]тЖТ 1:3-4 (W of M 1:1-11; 3 Ne 5:11-18; Hab 2:2; D&C 47:1-4)
- `doctrine:the-gifts-cease-through-the-peoples-unbelief-not-Gods-change` тАФ["the work of miracles and of healing did cease because of the iniquity of the people. And there were no gifts from the Lord, and the Holy Ghost did not come upon any, BECAUSE OF THEIR WICKEDNESS AND UNBELIEF"; the exact counterpart to Mormon's own 3 Ne 29 warning against cessationism тАФ God did NOT stop working by gifts (God changes not), the PEOPLE cut themselves off; gifts cease not because the heavens close from above but because hearts close from below; miracles still flow wherever faith opens the channel (Moro 7:35-37), dry up only where unbelief stops it; the variable was never God]тЖТ 1:13-14 (3 Ne 29:5-6; Morm 9:15-26; Moro 7:35-37; Mal 3:6)
- `doctrine:the-individual-of-a-sober-mind-is-visited-even-in-a-faithless-age` тАФ["I, being fifteen years of age and being somewhat of a sober mind, THEREFORE I was visited of the Lord, and tasted and knew of the goodness of Jesus"; in a generation from which the Holy Ghost had withdrawn and the gifts had ceased, one fifteen-year-old was visited and came to KNOW (not believe) the goodness of Jesus personally; the "therefore" works тАФ sober mind тЖТ visited; the gifts ceased GENERALLY for a people in unbelief, but the individual whose heart stayed sober and open could still taste; the hope buried in v14 тАФ the withdrawal from a wicked people does not seal off the faithful individual]тЖТ 1:15 (Ps 34:8; Alma 36:26; 1 Pet 2:3; 2 Ne 4:26)
- `doctrine:the-willing-preacher-forbidden-the-word-withdrawn-from-wilful-rebellion` тАФ[a converted, Lord-visited young man who wanted to share it "did endeavor to preach... but my mouth was shut, and I was forbidden... for behold they had wilfully rebelled against their God"; FORBIDDEN by the Lord, not men, "because of the hardness of their hearts"; a threshold of wilful rebellion past which the Lord withdraws even the OFFER of the word тАФ not arbitrary cruelty but the natural consequence of persistent rejection (the famine of hearing the word, Amos 8:11-12; Micah 3:6-7); stark contrast with 3 Ne 30's open door ("come unto me") тАФ a few generations of rebellion later the door is closed from the inside, even a willing missionary forbidden to knock; mercy keeps the door open as long as anyone reaches for it]тЖТ 1:16-17 (Amos 8:11-12; Micah 3:6-7; 1 Sam 3:1; 3 Ne 30:2)
- `theme:the-collapse-fulfills-the-prophets-Abinadi-and-Samuel-vindicated` тАФ[the Gadianton robbers infest, treasures "became slippery... that they could not hold them" (exactly Samuel's prophecy, Hel 13:18-37); sorceries/witchcrafts/magics spread "even unto the fulfilling of all the words of Abinadi, and also Samuel the Lamanite"; the collapse is not random but PROPHESIED, and its arrival vindicates the prophets killed or rejected for saying it would come тАФ Abinadi burned by Noah's priests, Samuel shot at on the wall, their words now coming true on the very people who rejected them; the fulfilled word is the witness (3 Ne 23, Hel 8:20-21), here terrible: the destruction itself proves the prophets right]тЖТ 1:18-19 (Hel 13:18-37; Mosiah 17:7-20; Hel 13-15; 3 Ne 23:9-13)

### from Mormon 2
- `doctrine:godly-sorrow-vs-the-sorrowing-of-the-damned` тАФ[the Nephites finally mourn, Mormon's heart rejoices supposing they'd become righteous тАФ but "this my joy was vain, for their sorrowing was NOT unto repentance, because of the goodness of God; but it was rather the SORROWING OF THE DAMNED, because the Lord would not always suffer them to take happiness in sin"; Paul's distinction (2 Cor 7:10) тАФ godly sorrow grieves the SIN ITSELF, drawn toward repentance by God's goodness; the sorrow of the world grieves only that the CONSEQUENCES hurt, that the sin can't be enjoyed; they didn't mourn betraying God, they mourned that God wouldn't let them be happy in sin тАФ frustrated appetite, not contrition]тЖТ 2:12-13 (2 Cor 7:10; Alma 42:29; Hosea 7:14; Alma 41:10)
- `doctrine:the-tell-is-the-direction-of-the-turn-toward-Christ-or-cursing-God` тАФ["they did not come unto Jesus with broken hearts and contrite spirits, but they did CURSE GOD, and wish to die"; the diagnostic of which sorrow it is тАФ godly sorrow turns TOWARD Christ (broken heart, contrite spirit, the only sacrifice He asks); the sorrowing of the damned turns AGAINST God, cursing Him because the source of the lost pleasure is correctly identified as God's refusal to let sin be happy; the same affliction softens one heart and hardens another, the direction of the turn reveals everything тАФ sorrow over consequences returns to the sin if consequences lift; sorrow over sin turns to Christ even if they remain]тЖТ 2:14 (3 Ne 9:20; Ps 51:17; 2 Ne 2:7; Rev 16:9-11)
- `doctrine:the-day-of-grace-can-pass-for-a-people-who-wilfully-harden` тАФ["I saw that the day of grace was passed with them, both temporally and spiritually; for I saw thousands of them hewn down in open rebellion against their God, and heaped up as dung upon the face of the land"; Jeremiah's lament made real (Jer 8:20, "the harvest is past, the summer is ended, and we are not saved"); NOT grace running out or God ceasing to offer, but the PEOPLE so wilfully hardened that the season in which the offer could take effect had closed тАФ grace still grace, they no longer soil it could grow in; "heaped up as dung" (Jer 8:2) deliberately dehumanizing тАФ what their chosen rebellion made of them]тЖТ 2:15 (Jer 8:20; Jer 8:1-3; Hel 13:38; Alma 34:32-35)
- `theme:the-prophets-lifelong-grief-and-unshaken-hope` тАФ["a continual scene of wickedness and abominations has been before mine eyes ever since I have been sufficient to behold the ways of man... my heart has been filled with sorrow because of their wickedness, ALL MY DAYS; nevertheless, I know that I shall be lifted up at the last day"; what it costs to be the righteous witness in a wicked age тАФ not occasional grief but a heart filled with sorrow all his days, a life spent watching what he loved destroy itself; yet not despair тАФ the deepest grief over his people held simultaneously with unshaken assurance of his own redemption; the anchor is what makes the sorrow bearable]тЖТ 2:18-19 (Mosiah 23:22; Ether 4:19; Morm 9:13; John 16:33)
- `doctrine:the-most-frightening-judgment-is-being-left-to-ourselves` тАФ["nevertheless the strength of the Lord was not with us; yea, we were left to ourselves, that the Spirit of the Lord did not abide in us; therefore we had become weak like unto our brethren"; the quiet horror beneath the war narrative тАФ the Nephites still WIN battles but by their own arm, not the Lord's strength; for a people whose history ran on "keep my commandments and prosper" (1 Ne 2:20), to be "left to ourselves" is the covenant's reversal тАФ not a thunderbolt but God's withdrawal, abandonment to their own resources; "weak like unto our brethren" тАФ the Nephite/Lamanite distinction collapsed, both now without the Spirit; the day of grace passing is at bottom the Spirit ceasing to abide]тЖТ 2:26 (1 Ne 2:20; Hel 4:24-26; Mosiah 1:13; Judg 16:20)
- `theme:the-boy-trusted-with-their-bodies-refused-with-their-souls` тАФ[at sixteen, "large in stature," Mormon made commander of the entire Nephite army тАФ a boy bearing the weight of leading a dying civilization in total war; the Lord visited him at 15, forbade him to preach (1:16-17), and now the people who would not hear him preach hand him their armies; he can lead them in war but not call them to repentance, they'll follow him into battle but not to Christ; trusted with their bodies and refused with their souls тАФ the whole tragedy of his life in that contrast]тЖТ 2:1-2 (Morm 1:16-17; Alma 43:17; 1 Sam 17:33)

### from Mormon 3
- `doctrine:the-Lord-renews-the-offer-of-mercy-even-past-the-day-of-grace` тАФ[Mormon had seen "the day of grace was passed" (2:15), yet the Lord commands him to cry repentance AGAIN: "come unto me, and be ye baptized, and build up again my church, and ye shall be spared"; the Lord's mercy outruns even the prophet's grim assessment тАФ as long as there is breath the offer is renewed; but the cry was "in vain"]тЖТ 3:2 (Hel 15:16-17; Morm 6:11-15; 2 Pet 3:9; Matt 23:37)
- `doctrine:ingratitude-is-failing-to-perceive-that-it-was-the-Lord-who-spared-you` тАФ["they did not realize that it was the Lord that had spared them, and granted unto them a chance for repentance"; every deliverance, every quiet decade between wars, was God holding the door open, and they read it as their own fortune or strength; ingratitude is not merely failing to say thanks but failing to PERCEIVE THE SOURCE тАФ to see God's hand in the very mercies that should have turned them; a people who cannot recognize when they are being spared cannot repent, because they don't know there is anything to repent toward]тЖТ 3:3 (Neh 9:16-17; Deut 8:17-18; Hosea 2:8; Luke 17:17-18)
- `doctrine:boasting-in-own-strength-and-the-vengeance-oath-cross-from-defensive-to-offensive-war` тАФ[after two defensive victories, "because of this great thing which my people had done, they began to boast in their own strength" (not "the Lord delivered us" but "look what we did") "and began to swear before the heavens that they would avenge themselves... and cut them off from the face of the land"; two compounding sins тАФ boasting (crediting their own arm for the Lord's mercy) and the vengeance-OATH ("by the throne of God," forbidden oaths, 3 Ne 12:34) to go on the OFFENSIVE; this crosses the bright line of centuries тАФ war permitted only in defense, never to give offense (Alma 48:14); they became the aggressors, swearing by God's throne to do what God forbids]тЖТ 3:9-10 (Alma 48:14; Alma 43:46-47; 3 Ne 12:34; D&C 98:33-38)
- `doctrine:Mormon-refuses-to-lead-conscientious-objection-love-without-faith` тАФ["I, Mormon, did utterly refuse from this time forth to be a commander... because of their wickedness" тАФ the general who led them since sixteen resigns rather than lead an offensive war of vengeance; conscientious objection at the highest level, refusing to participate in evil even when done by his own people, even at the cost of leaving them leaderless; NOT a refusal of love тАФ "I had loved them... with all my heart; and my soul had been poured out in prayer... all the day long for them; nevertheless, it was without faith, because of the hardness of their hearts"; he prayed as one prays for the dying he loves but knows will not recover тАФ prayer real, love real, faith impossible against their hardness]тЖТ 3:11-12 (Morm 5:1-2; James 1:6; Hel 10:4-5; Jer 7:16)
- `doctrine:vengeance-is-mine-usurping-Gods-vengeance-is-the-final-sin` тАФ["Vengeance is mine, and I will repay; and because this people repented not after I had delivered them, behold, they shall be cut off"; the vengeance-oath was USURPATION тАФ vengeance belongs to God alone (Deut 32:35, Rom 12:19), not because it's wrong in the absolute but because only perfect justice and perfect knowledge can be trusted with it; for a man to swear vengeance "by the throne of God" is to claim a prerogative that is God's, to sit in His seat; the Lord's response is not "I forbid it" but more terrible тАФ very well, vengeance is mine, and I will repay it upon YOU; the usurpation of God's vengeance becomes the occasion of God's vengeance]тЖТ 3:14-15 (Deut 32:35; Rom 12:19; D&C 82:23; Heb 10:30)
- `doctrine:the-idle-witness-when-you-cannot-fix-it-witness-truthfully` тАФ["I did stand as an idle witness to manifest unto the world the things which I saw and heard"; from commander to WITNESS тАФ "idle" exact and startling, he does nothing militarily, stands aside, watches; but not passivity for its own sake тАФ he stands idle precisely to "manifest unto the world the things which I saw and heard"; the sober child "quick to observe" (1:2) comes full circle тАФ his life's work was never the army but the record; when he could no longer lead them in righteousness he could still witness them truthfully for us; sometimes the faithful act is not to keep fighting a losing battle but to witness truthfully, so those who come after can learn what you couldn't make your contemporaries learn]тЖТ 3:16 (Morm 1:2; 3 Ne 5:11-18; Ezek 3:17; Hab 2:2)
- `doctrine:the-Book-of-Mormon-is-the-other-witness-that-Jesus-is-the-very-God` тАФ["that the Jews, the covenant people of the Lord, shall have OTHER WITNESS besides him whom they saw and heard, that Jesus, whom they slew, was the very Christ and the very GOD"; the Book of Mormon is the second witness to the divinity of Christ тАФ and note the doubled claim, not merely "the very Christ" (Messiah/anointed) but "the very GOD"; Mormon, like Nephi/Abinadi/Moroni, places Jesus squarely in identity with God; the whole point of the record he is "idle witness" to is to add a second witness across an ocean and fifteen centuries to the testimony the Jews rejected: that the Jesus they slew was God]тЖТ 3:21 (2 Ne 25:18; 2 Ne 26:12; Mosiah 7:27; 3 Ne 28:10-11)
- `theme:the-idle-witness-is-the-most-active-missionary-reaching-past-his-own-people-to-the-reader` тАФ[from the dying Nephites Mormon turns and speaks straight to US тАФ "I write unto you, Gentiles, and also unto you, house of Israel... unto you, twelve tribes of Israel"; the judgment structure (twelve tribes by the Jerusalem Twelve, the Nephite remnant by the Nephite Twelve who are judged by the Jerusalem Twelve), the universal reach ("every soul who belongs to the whole human family of Adam"), and the yearning "I would that I could persuade all ye ends of the earth to repent"; even as his own people march to destruction, his heart reaches every future reader тАФ the idle witness is, in the act of writing, the most active missionary of all]тЖТ 3:17-22 (1 Ne 12:9-10; 3 Ne 27:27; Alma 29:1-2; Moro 10:32)

### from Mormon 4
- `doctrine:the-offensive-war-strips-the-defense-the-aggression-itself-makes-them-vulnerable` тАФ["it was because the armies of the Nephites went up unto the Lamanites that they began to be smitten; for were it not for that, the Lamanites could have had no power over them"; the direct consequence of ch 3's vengeance-oath тАФ the moment they abandoned the defensive ground (the only ground a covenant people may fight on, Alma 48:14) and went UP on the offensive, they forfeited their protection; precise counterfactual тАФ had they stayed defensive they could not have been beaten; the turn to vengeance doesn't make a people stronger, it makes them vulnerable, severing them from the only strength that was ever theirs]тЖТ 4:4 (Morm 3:9-15; Alma 48:14; D&C 98:33-38; Alma 43:46-47)
- `doctrine:it-is-by-the-wicked-that-the-wicked-are-punished` тАФ["the judgments of God will overtake the wicked; and it is by the wicked that the wicked are punished; for it is the wicked that stir up the hearts of the children of men unto bloodshed"; Mormon's theology of how judgment actually works тАФ not thunderbolts but God LETTING SIN RUN ITS COURSE, and the course sin runs is self-destruction; the Lamanites (wicked) punish the Nephites (wicked) and vice versa, the wicked at once punishers and punished because wickedness is self-consuming; God needn't import external punishment for a people fully given to evil тАФ their evil punishes them through each other; answers how God can use wicked Lamanites to punish wicked Nephites тАФ He's not endorsing them, permitting wickedness to do what it does, the instrument as guilty as the target]тЖТ 4:5 (Nahum 1:3; 2 Pet 2:12; D&C 63:33; Judg 7:22)
- `doctrine:the-final-hardening-is-delighting-in-the-shedding-of-blood` тАФ["every heart was hardened, so that they DELIGHTED in the shedding of blood continually. And there never had been so great wickedness among all the children of Lehi, nor even among all the house of Israel... as was among this people"; the final stage of hardening is not merely tolerating bloodshed but DELIGHTING in it тАФ violence become pleasure, the conscience so dead that killing is enjoyed; worse than anyone in all Israel's history; the cross-ref is Gen 6:5 (the wickedness before the Flood, "only evil continually") тАФ Noah-level corruption, the kind that precedes total destruction]тЖТ 4:11-12 (Gen 6:5; Moses 7:36-37; 3 Ne 9:9; Moro 9:5, 19-20)
- `theme:the-sacrifice-of-innocents-and-the-cycle-of-rage-not-repentance` тАФ[women and children "offer[ed] up as sacrifices unto their idol gods" (the detail recurs тАФ it had become routine), the deepest pit of idolatry (Jer 19:5, the valley of Hinnom; Abr 1:8); and the Nephite response is its own indictment тАФ when their women and children were sacrificed they went "with exceedingly great anger," not with repentance or grief that turned them to God but with RAGE; the slaughter of innocents hardened them further toward vengeance instead of softening them toward heaven; a people who answer atrocity only with greater fury, never with "why has God's protection left us?", are past softening; the cycle of vengeance the Lord forbade (3:15) running to its end]тЖТ 4:14-15, 21 (Jer 19:5; Abr 1:8; 2 Kgs 17:31; Lev 18:21)
- `image:swept-off-even-as-a-dew-before-the-sun` тАФ["the Nephites gain no power over the Lamanites, but began to be swept off by them even as a dew before the sun"; after all the boasting in their own strength, not a heroic last stand but EVAPORATION тАФ swept away as effortlessly as the rising sun burns off the morning dew, gone without a struggle, leaving no trace; a people who would not be gathered as Christ longed to gather them ("as a hen gathereth her chickens", 3 Ne 10:4-6) are now swept away as dew; they would not be gathered, so they are swept off тАФ both verbs of being-acted-upon]тЖТ 4:18 (3 Ne 10:4-6; Matt 23:37; Hosea 13:3; Ps 1:4)
- `theme:the-record-walks-out-of-the-collapse-alive` тАФ["now I, Mormon, seeing that the Lamanites were about to overthrow the land, therefore I did go to the hill Shim, and did take up all the records which Ammaron had hid up unto the Lord"; as his civilization evaporates Mormon does the one thing that will outlast it тАФ secures the full archive (all the sacred records, not just the plates of Nephi he took earlier); the "idle witness" made concrete тАФ he can't save his people but can save the record of them, for us; something quietly heroic in walking to a hill to gather books while the world burns, because the books will reach a people the swords never could; everything else swept off as dew, the record the one thing that survives тАФ the testimony walks out alive in Mormon's arms]тЖТ 4:23 (Morm 2:17; 4 Ne 1:48-49; W of M 1:3; 3 Ne 5:11-18)

### from Mormon 5
- `doctrine:leading-without-hope-fidelity-without-expectation-of-victory` тАФ[Mormon "did repent of the oath" and takes command again "for they looked upon me as though I could deliver them" тАФ but "I was WITHOUT HOPE, for I knew the judgments of the Lord which should come upon them"; he returns to lead a people he KNOWS are doomed, not expecting victory or repentance but because they look to him and he loves them and someone must stand at their head as they die; the man who refused to lead them into evil (3:11) will lead them into a death he cannot prevent, because leading them in their last extremity is not evil but love without illusion; the detail that seals it тАФ "they repented not... but did struggle for their lives without calling upon that Being who created them" тАФ the will to live without the willingness to repent]тЖТ 5:1-2 (Morm 3:11-12; Morm 2:19; John 10:11-15; Esther 4:16)
- `doctrine:the-record-comes-forth-to-persuade-that-Jesus-is-the-Christ-and-to-gather-Israel` тАФ["that they may be persuaded that Jesus is the Christ, the Son of the living God; that the Father may bring about... his great and eternal purpose, in restoring the Jews, or all the house of Israel, to the land of their inheritance... unto the fulfilling of his covenant"; two intertwined purposes тАФ to PERSUADE (that Jesus is the Christ, the Son of the living God, the same doubled divine claim as 3:21) and to GATHER (restore Israel, fulfill the Abrahamic covenant); the book is both a witness of Christ and an instrument of the gathering тАФ conversion and covenant are not separate works but one]тЖТ 5:14 (2 Ne 25:16-17; John 20:31; Morm 3:21; 3 Ne 16:11-12)
- `doctrine:the-mercy-in-the-editing-truth-told-but-the-full-horror-spared` тАФ["I, Mormon, do not desire to harrow up the souls of men in casting before them such an awful scene of blood and carnage... therefore I write a small abridgment, daring not to give a full account... that ye might not have too great sorrow because of the wickedness of this people"; even the record-keeper exercises mercy in the editing тАФ tells the truth but spares the reader the full weight of the horror (the same forbearance as 2:18); the abridgment is itself an act of compassion toward the future reader]тЖТ 5:8-9 (Morm 2:18; 3 Ne 26:6-12; John 21:25; Matt 10:26)
- `bin4:dark-filthy-loathsome-because-of-unbelief-and-idolatry` тАФ["this people shall be scattered, and shall become a dark, a filthy, and a loathsome people, beyond the description of that which ever hath been amongst us, yea, even that which hath been among the Lamanites, and this BECAUSE OF THEIR UNBELIEF AND IDOLATRY"; same complex as 2 Ne 5:21; honest observations: the CAUSE is explicitly named (unbelief + idolatry, a spiritual condition not ancestry); "dark" sits in a triad with "filthy" + "loathsome" (moral/spiritual descriptors); said of the NEPHITE seed тАФ the once-"delightsome" covenant people (v17) тАФ who fall WORSE than the Lamanites ever were (the favored fall further than the cursed); cross-ref "become"тЖТ2 Ne 26:33 (all alike unto God); all points to a spiritual state, but the literal "dark" remains unreconciled residue тАФ FLAGGED FOR MICHAEL + THE SPIRIT, NOT resolved by the agent]тЖТ 5:15 (2 Ne 5:21; Alma 3:6-19; 2 Ne 26:33; 4 Ne 1:17, 38)
- `doctrine:the-Spirit-ceasing-to-strive-leaves-a-people-as-chaff-and-a-rudderless-ship` тАФ["the Spirit of the Lord hath already ceased to strive with their fathers... they were once a delightsome people, and they had Christ for their shepherd; yea, they were led even by God the Father. But now... they are led about by Satan, even as chaff is driven before the wind, or as a vessel is tossed about upon the waves, without sail or anchor"; two images, both LOSS OF DIRECTION тАФ chaff has no will of its own, goes wherever the wind takes it (Ps 1:4); the rudderless ship is tossed by every wave, going nowhere it chooses; the Spirit's withdrawal is not merely the absence of a feeling but the loss of all bearings; the freedom they thought they seized by throwing off God is the opposite тАФ to be without the Spirit is to be chaff, a ship no one steers (Eph 4:14)]тЖТ 5:16-18 (Gen 6:3; Ps 1:4; Hosea 13:3; Eph 4:14)
- `doctrine:the-covenant-outlasts-the-fall-the-Lord-remembers-after-the-scattering` тАФ["after they have been driven and scattered by the Gentiles, behold, THEN will the Lord remember the covenant which he made unto Abraham and unto all the house of Israel"; the scattering is not the last word тАФ there is a "then": after the driving, after centuries as chaff, the Lord remembers the Abrahamic covenant and the remnant is gathered; the covenant is not voided by the people's unbelief, it waits on God's side to be fulfilled "in his own due time"; God's faithfulness outlasts the people's faithlessness]тЖТ 5:19-20 (1 Ne 13:31; 3 Ne 16:11; Rom 11:25-29; Lev 26:42)
- `doctrine:the-prayers-of-the-righteous-are-banked-and-answered-generations-later` тАФ["the Lord will remember the prayers of the righteous, which have been put up unto him for them"; the prayers of the faithful dead тАФ Enos pleading for the Lamanites' preservation (Enos 1:12-18), generations of prophets praying for a people who would not listen тАФ are BANKED, remembered by God, answered long after the ones who prayed have died; a prayer offered in faith for a wayward people is not wasted even if that generation never repents тАФ held by God and brought to bear on their seed centuries later; the righteous who prayed for the Lamanites didn't see the answer, but it's coming, through this very record, to their distant descendants]тЖТ 5:21 (Enos 1:12-18; Morm 8:24-26; Morm 9:36-37; Rev 8:3-4)
- `theme:the-Gentiles-are-warned-they-too-are-in-the-hands-of-God` тАФ["O ye Gentiles, how can ye stand before the power of God, except ye shall repent and turn from your evil ways? Know ye not that ye are in the hands of God?... lest a remnant of the seed of Jacob shall go forth among you as a lion, and tear you in pieces, and there is none to deliver"; the Gentiles are not spectators to the tragedy but participants under the same terms тАФ they'll scatter the remnant, possess the land, receive the record, and they too must repent or face the lion (3 Ne 20:16); the covenant cuts both ways тАФ no possessing the land of promise on easier terms than the Nephites had; the idle witness ends his explanation of why the record exists by warning the very people who'll hold it]тЖТ 5:22-24 (3 Ne 20:16; 3 Ne 21:12-13; Micah 5:8; D&C 87:6)

### from Mormon 6
- `doctrine:the-record-secured-at-the-moment-of-national-death-the-priority-that-outlasts-everything` тАФ["I made this record out of the plates of Nephi, and hid up in the hill Cumorah all the records which had been entrusted to me... save it were these few plates which I gave unto my son Moroni"; the hinge of the whole Book of Mormon's survival тАФ Mormon separates the archive (full set hidden in Cumorah, abridgment given to Moroni who'll finish it and from whom Joseph Smith receives it, D&C 128:20); at the very moment of national death, with his ten thousand about to die under his command, his last administrative act is to ensure the RECORD survives; the bodies would molder, the testimony would reach a people across an ocean and a millennium тАФ he understood what mattered]тЖТ 6:6 (D&C 128:20; JS-H 1:52; Morm 8:1-4; Moro 10:2)
- `theme:the-roll-call-of-the-ten-thousands-refuses-to-let-the-dead-be-a-statistic` тАФ[from the top of the hill Mormon counts the dead not as a number but by NAME тАФ "the ten thousand of Gidgiddonah had fallen... Lamah... Gilgal... Limhah... Jeneum... Cumenihah, Moronihah, Antionum, Shiblom, Shem, Josh, had fallen with their ten thousand each... ten more"; twenty-three named ten-thousands plus Mormon's and Moroni's тАФ over 200,000 dead; the agony is the naming тАФ he names the captains, each a man he knew, each leading ten thousand more; the roll call refuses to let the dead be a statistic, every name a man; then even the names strip away тАФ "their flesh, and bones, and blood lay upon the face of the earth... to molder upon the land"]тЖТ 6:11-15 (1 Ne 12:19; Alma 45:11-14; 2 Sam 1:19; Judg 1:4)
- `doctrine:the-tragedy-was-avoidable-Jesus-stood-with-open-arms` тАФ["O ye fair ones, how could ye have rejected that Jesus, who STOOD WITH OPEN ARMS to receive you! Behold, if ye had not done this, ye would not have fallen"; the deepest sorrow тАФ not that they died but that they need not have, because Jesus stood the whole time with open arms (His own image: "his arms of mercy are extended... and they will not", 2 Ne 26:7; "how oft would I have gathered you... and ye would not", 3 Ne 10:5); they fell not because God abandoned them or fate decreed it but because they turned from open arms; the whole catastrophe was AVOIDABLE тАФ that is what makes it unbearable; every moldering body could have been clasped in the arms of Jesus]тЖТ 6:17-18 (2 Ne 26:7; 3 Ne 9:14; 3 Ne 10:4-6; Matt 23:37)
- `theme:the-dead-grieved-as-families-not-combatants` тАФ["O ye fair sons and daughters, ye fathers and mothers, ye husbands and wives, ye fair ones, how is it that ye could have fallen!"; the litany makes the dead human in a way the ten-thousands could not тАФ not soldiers in the abstract but FAMILIES, sons and daughters, fathers and mothers, husbands and wives; the relationships named one by one because that is what was destroyed тАФ not an army but a web of love, every bond severed by the sword; and the helplessness every grief knows тАФ "ye are gone, and my sorrows cannot bring your return"; the prophet who could lead armies cannot bring back one of the dead]тЖТ 6:19-20 (Lam 2:11; Jer 9:1; 2 Sam 18:33; John 11:35)
- `doctrine:the-lament-turns-to-the-resurrection-and-the-judgment` тАФ["the day soon cometh that your mortal must put on immortality, and these bodies which are now moldering in corruption must soon become incorruptible bodies; and then ye must stand before the judgment-seat of Christ... and if it so be that ye are righteous, then are ye blessed"; from the moldering bodies Mormon lifts his eyes to the resurrection (1 Cor 15:53-54) тАФ the bodies crumbling into the earth will rise; the dead judged "according to their works," but Mormon does NOT pronounce their doom тАФ he leaves the door open ("if it so be that ye are righteous"); even of a people destroyed for wickedness he will not presume to declare them lost, the judgment is Christ's not his]тЖТ 6:21 (1 Cor 15:53-54; Alma 11:43-45; 3 Ne 27:14-16; Mosiah 16:10)
- `doctrine:committing-the-dead-to-God-who-knows-their-state-and-acts-in-justice-and-mercy` тАФ["O that ye had repented before this great destruction had come upon you. But behold, ye are gone, and the Father, yea, the Eternal Father of heaven, KNOWETH YOUR STATE; and he doeth with you according to his justice and mercy"; Mormon hands his dead to God тАФ he doesn't know their eternal fate and doesn't claim to, but knows two things about the God who does: God KNOWS their state (every heart, every degree of light they had) and acts "according to his justice AND mercy" (not justice alone which would terrify, not mercy alone which would be sentimental, but both perfectly held); after watching his people destroy themselves by rejecting Christ, his last word over their bodies is a word of TRUST; where a faithful man lands when he's done all he could and it wasn't enough тАФ not despair, not presumption, but committing the unbearable to a God he trusts with both justice and mercy]тЖТ 6:22 (Alma 42:15; Ps 36:5-6; Alma 26:16; D&C 6:16)

### from Mormon 7
- `doctrine:the-dying-prophets-last-words-bless-the-descendants-of-his-enemies` тАФ[Mormon's record ends not with his own annihilated people but addressing "the remnant of this people who are spared" тАФ the descendants of the Lamanites who destroyed his nation тАФ and blessing them; not one syllable of bitterness, not one curse, not one word of vengeance; the man whose whole civilization the Lamanites annihilated spends his last words trying to SAVE the Lamanites' children; love of enemies carried to its furthest extreme; mirrors the Savior's close in 3 Ne 30 ("come unto me") тАФ Mormon sounds exactly like the Christ he witnessed, the door held open even to those who did the killing]тЖТ 7:1-2 (3 Ne 30:1-2; Matt 5:44; Luke 23:34; Alma 24:17-19)
- `doctrine:identity-comes-first-know-ye-that-ye-are-of-the-house-of-Israel` тАФ["Know ye that ye are of the house of Israel" тАФ before repentance, before belief, before anything, know who you ARE; these Lamanites who have no idea they are covenant people, taught for centuries to hate the Nephites, are in fact the remnant of Jacob, heirs of the Abrahamic covenant; Mormon begins not with their sin but with their belonging тАФ you cannot call a people home until they know they have a home; the first gift is the knowledge of their own identity]тЖТ 7:2, 10 (Hel 15:11-13; 1 Ne 5:14; Alma 10:3; Eph 2:12-19)
- `doctrine:lay-down-your-weapons-delight-no-more-in-the-shedding-of-blood` тАФ["ye must lay down your weapons of war, and delight no more in the shedding of blood, and take them not again, save it be that God shall command you"; pointed precisely at the sin that destroyed both peoples (the delight in bloodshed, 4:11); Mormon the lifelong general who came to hate the war he was good at tells the survivors to lay it down; the only exception is defensive war at God's command (Alma 43:47); the renunciation of violence is not incidental to the gospel he preaches but near its center, because violence is what he watched consume everyone he loved]тЖТ 7:4 (Alma 43:47; D&C 98:33-37; Isa 2:4; Micah 4:3)
- `doctrine:the-compressed-gospel-Son-of-God-slain-risen-victor-over-the-grave` тАФ["believe in Jesus Christ, that he is the Son of God, and that he was slain by the Jews, and by the power of the Father he hath risen again, whereby he hath gained the victory over the grave; and also in him is the sting of death swallowed up... he bringeth to pass the resurrection... the redemption of the world"; the whole gospel in three sentences тАФ divine sonship, death, resurrection, victory over the grave (the "sting of death swallowed up", Paul's triumph 1 Cor 15:54-55 from Isa 25:8), universal resurrection, judgment, redemption; the destiny of the guiltless in language of pure joy тАФ "to sing ceaseless praises with the choirs above... in a state of happiness which hath no end"; he holds out to the children of bloodshed a destiny of song]тЖТ 7:5-7 (1 Cor 15:54-55; Isa 25:8; 2 Ne 9:6-13; Alma 11:42-45)
- `doctrine:the-Father-Son-and-Holy-Ghost-are-one-God` тАФ["to sing ceaseless praises with the choirs above, unto the Father, and unto the Son, and unto the Holy Ghost, WHICH ARE ONE GOD, in a state of happiness which hath no end"; the doubled witness again тАФ three named, one God (Deut 6:4; D&C 20:28); Mormon's farewell, like his statement of the record's purpose (3:21, 5:14), affirms the oneness of the Godhead]тЖТ 7:7 (Deut 6:4; Gal 3:20; D&C 20:28; 3 Ne 11:27, 36)
- `doctrine:the-Bible-and-the-Book-of-Mormon-are-mutual-witnesses` тАФ["lay hold upon the gospel of Christ... not only in this record but also in the record which shall come unto the Gentiles from the Jews... this is written for the intent that ye may believe THAT; and if ye believe THAT ye will believe THIS also"; two records тАФ the Bible (from the Jews, through the Gentiles) and the Book of Mormon (this record, also through the Gentiles); the reciprocal logic тАФ each written to lead to the other; the BoM exists to confirm the Bible, and belief in the Bible opens to belief in the BoM; not rivals but mutual witnesses, each establishing the other's truth (2 Ne 29:8, two nations two witnesses; 1 Ne 13:40); the answer to the false dichotomy тАФ the BoM doesn't replace or compete with the Bible, it was written so people would believe the Bible]тЖТ 7:8-9 (2 Ne 29:8; 1 Ne 13:38-41; Ezek 37:15-19; John 5:39)
- `theme:it-shall-be-well-with-you-the-last-word-is-blessing-not-lament` тАФ["if it so be that ye believe in Christ, and are baptized, first with water, then with fire and with the Holy Ghost, following the example of our Savior... it shall be well with you in the day of judgment. Amen"; Mormon's whole record closes on identity + path + promise woven together тАФ the last thing he writes is not a lament (though he had every reason) or a curse (though his people lay slaughtered) but a BENEDICTION over his enemies' descendants тАФ "it shall be well with you"; the whole arc of his life тАФ sober child, boy general, idle witness, grieving father тАФ resolves into hope held out to the future, even from the ashes; he could not save his own people, he gave everything to save the people his record would one day reach]тЖТ 7:10 (3 Ne 19:13; 2 Ne 31:13-14; Matt 3:11; Moro 10:32)

### from Mormon 8
- `doctrine:Moroni-alone-faithfulness-when-every-external-reason-for-hope-is-gone` тАФ["I, Moroni... even remain alone to write the sad tale of the destruction of my people... I have not friends nor whither to go; and how long the Lord will suffer that I may live I know not. And whether they will slay me, I know not"; the loneliest voice in scripture тАФ the last man of a people that numbered like the sands, writing into the dark for readers he cannot see, with no guarantee he'll finish or survive the night; a particular faithfulness the rest of us rarely summon тАФ to do the work you were given when every external reason for hope is gone, no community, no certainty of tomorrow; kept going by nothing but the commandment and the love of God]тЖТ 8:1-5 (Moro 1:1-3; Moro 9:22; Ether 4:3; 2 Tim 4:16-17)
- `doctrine:the-record-is-imperfect-but-true-condemn-it-not-the-faults-are-mens` тАФ["whoso receiveth this record, and shall not condemn it because of the imperfections which are in it, the same shall know of greater things... if there be faults they be the faults of a man... nevertheless God knoweth all things; therefore, he that condemneth, let him be aware lest he shall be in danger of hell fire"; a stunning posture for a prophet writing scripture тАФ he does NOT claim the record is flawless, he claims it is TRUE; the condition of receiving its greater things is humility, the willingness not to dismiss it over its human faults; the faults are the writer's, the truth is God's; the reader who condemns it over its human imperfections endangers himself]тЖТ 8:12, 17 (3 Ne 5:15-18; Ether 12:23-28; Moro 9:31; 1 Ne 19:6)
- `doctrine:the-plates-are-worthless-the-record-is-priceless-not-for-gain` тАФ["the plates thereof are of no worth... but the record thereof is of great worth; and whoso shall bring it to light, him will the Lord bless... God wills that it shall be done with an eye single to his glory"; the gold is worthless, the words are priceless; anyone seeking the plates "to get gain" will be disappointed (the warning Moroni would later give Joseph Smith, JS-H 1:53) тАФ the treasure was never the metal; "it shall be brought out of darkness unto light... out of the earth... by the power of God" тАФ a book buried by the last man of a dead people will rise from the ground 14 centuries later, and Moroni alone with the plates knows it]тЖТ 8:14-16 (JS-H 1:53; 2 Ne 3:7; D&C 4:5; 3 Ne 21:11)
- `doctrine:the-eternal-purposes-of-the-Lord-roll-on-the-work-cannot-be-stopped` тАФ["the eternal purposes of the Lord shall roll on, until all his promises shall be fulfilled"; the bedrock under the chapter тАФ nothing can stop the work, not the destruction of the Nephites, not the burial of the record, not those who "breathe out wrath and strifes against the work of the Lord" and say "We will destroy the work of the Lord" (in danger of being hewn down); the work of God cannot be frustrated (D&C 3:1-3); Moroni, who just watched his entire civilization destroyed and has every reason to conclude God's purposes CAN be defeated, declares the opposite from the ruins тАФ the destruction was a chapter in the work, not its defeat; from inside the total wreckage he sees the wreckage is not the end of the story]тЖТ 8:21-22 (D&C 3:1-3; Isa 14:24-27; Dan 2:44; 1 Ne 22:16-17)
- `doctrine:the-record-speaks-from-the-dust-as-if-one-should-speak-from-the-dead` тАФ["those saints who have gone before me... shall cry, yea, even from the dust will they cry unto the Lord... it shall come even as if one should speak from the dead"; the voice from the dust of Isaiah 29:4 тАФ the destroyed people crying a warning to the living; the record IS this тАФ a dead nation's voice rising from the ground to warn the people walking the same road; the prayers of the dead saints were banked for the future, "in behalf of him that the Lord should suffer to bring these things forth" (they prayed for the future translator)]тЖТ 8:23-26 (Isa 29:4; 2 Ne 26:16; 2 Ne 33:13; Enos 1:12-18)
- `doctrine:Moroni-was-shown-our-day-and-addresses-us-directly` тАФ["Behold, I speak unto you as if ye were present, and yet ye are not. But behold, JESUS CHRIST HATH SHOWN YOU UNTO ME, and I know your doing"; the most direct prophet-to-reader moment in scripture тАФ Moroni, alone in the ruins, was shown the latter-day reader by Christ, by name and deed ("I know your doing"), and wrote TO people he was shown in vision 15 centuries before they'd be born; the book is not a generic message that happens to apply to us тАФ it was written by a man shown our faces and our deeds, addressing us directly; reading Mormon 8 is reading a letter written specifically to us by someone who saw us]тЖТ 8:34-35 (2 Ne 27:6-22; D&C 3:16; Isa 29:11-18; John 17:20)
- `doctrine:the-indictment-of-our-day-is-pride-and-very-fine-apparel` тАФ["I know that ye do walk in the pride of your hearts; and there are none save a few only who do not lift themselves up in the pride of their hearts, unto the wearing of very fine apparel... and your churches, yea, even every one, have become polluted because of the pride of your hearts"; the same pride that destroyed the Nephites and began the fall of Zion through "costly apparel" (4 Ne 1:24); Moroni sees it in us and sees it as nearly universal тАФ "none save a few only"; "very fine apparel" the marker again, the visible display of class and self-exaltation the BoM names as the entry point of pride]тЖТ 8:36 (4 Ne 1:24; Jacob 2:13; Alma 5:53; 2 Ne 28:11-14)
- `doctrine:the-measuring-line-loving-money-and-adornment-more-than-the-poor` тАФ["ye do love money, and your substance, and your fine apparel, and the adorning of your churches, MORE THAN ye love the poor and the needy, the sick and the afflicted... why do ye adorn yourselves with that which hath no life, and yet suffer the hungry, and the needy, and the naked, and the sick and the afflicted to pass by you, and notice them not?"; THE test the whole Book of Mormon returns to тАФ not what we profess or how we adorn our worship but whether we love our possessions more than the poor; Moroni's vision of the latter-day church is not heresy in the abstract but a concrete failure тАФ beautiful buildings, fine clothes, full accounts, and the suffering living passing by unnoticed; we adorn the LIFELESS (gold, cloth, buildings) while ignoring the living who suffer; the indictment of US from a man who watched a civilization die of this disease]тЖТ 8:37, 39 (Jacob 2:17-19; Mosiah 4:16-26; Alma 34:28-29; Matt 25:42-45)

### from Mormon 9
- `doctrine:hell-is-the-misery-of-the-unclean-soul-in-the-presence-of-holiness` тАФ["ye would be MORE MISERABLE to dwell with a holy and just God, under a consciousness of your filthiness before him, than ye would to dwell with the damned souls in hell... your nakedness before God, and also the glory of God, and the holiness of Jesus Christ... will kindle a flame of unquenchable fire upon you"; hell is not primarily a place God sends people to torture them but the unbearable misery of an unclean soul in the presence of perfect holiness тАФ the wicked placed in heaven would be in agony; the FIRE is the consciousness of guilt itself, burning hotter the brighter the holiness it stands before (exactly Alma's experience, Alma 36:14); the damned could not BEAR His presence, and that inability is the punishment; so the gospel is not God lowering a bar but God CHANGING the soul so it can finally bear, even delight in, the holiness it once couldn't endure]тЖТ 9:3-5 (Alma 36:12-16; 2 Ne 9:14-16; Rev 6:16; Alma 12:14)
- `doctrine:a-god-who-changes-is-no-God-immutability-is-deity` тАФ["God is the same yesterday, today, and forever, and in him there is no variableness neither shadow of changing... if ye have imagined up unto yourselves a god who doth vary... then have ye imagined up unto yourselves a god who is not a God of miracles"; the premise of the whole anti-cessationism argument тАФ a variable god is by definition a false one (Heb 13:8; Jas 1:17); immutability is not a peripheral attribute but constitutive of deity itself]тЖТ 9:9-10 (Heb 13:8; Jas 1:17; 1 Ne 10:18; Moro 8:18; D&C 20:12)
- `doctrine:God-still-works-miracles-because-He-changes-not` тАФ[the clean syllogism тАФ "if there were miracles wrought then, why has God ceased to be a God of miracles and yet be an unchangeable Being? And behold, I say unto you he changeth not; if so he would cease to be God; and he ceaseth not to be God, and is a God of miracles"; God doesn't change; God once worked miracles (creation itself, 9:17; Christ's works, the apostles', 9:18); therefore God still works miracles тАФ to say He stopped is to say He changed, and a God who changes is no God; cessationism doesn't merely deny a doctrine, it denies the IMMUTABILITY of God, and with it His deity; the climax of the argument running through Morm 1:13-14 + 3 Ne 29:6]тЖТ 9:15-19 (3 Ne 29:6; Morm 1:13-14; Moro 7:35-37; Gen 1:1)
- `doctrine:miracles-cease-only-because-people-dwindle-in-unbelief` тАФ["the reason why he ceaseth to do miracles among the children of men is BECAUSE THAT THEY DWINDLE IN UNBELIEF, and depart from the right way, and know not the God in whom they should trust"; the resolution the whole section built toward тАФ miracles DO cease, but not because God changed, because PEOPLE change, faith withers, a generation dwindles in unbelief; the variable is never God, it is always us; the heavens are not closed from above but shuttered from below; the corollary full of hope тАФ where faith returns so do the miracles ("whoso believeth in Christ, doubting nothing... shall be granted"); the gifts didn't expire with the apostles, they wait on God's unchanging side for the faith that can receive them]тЖТ 9:20-21 (Morm 1:13-14; 3 Ne 29:6; Moro 7:37; Ether 12:12)
- `doctrine:signs-follow-those-who-believe-doubting-nothing` тАФ["these signs shall follow them that believe тАФ in my name shall they cast out devils; they shall speak with new tongues... they shall lay hands on the sick and they shall recover... whosoever shall believe in my name, DOUBTING NOTHING, unto him will I confirm all my words"; Christ's own commission (Mark 16:15-18); the condition is always the same тАФ believe, doubting nothing; the signs FOLLOW the faith, they do not precede it or substitute for it; faith doubting nothing unlocks the gifts]тЖТ 9:21-25 (Mark 16:15-18; Matt 21:22; 3 Ne 18:20; Moro 7:33)
- `doctrine:the-fixity-of-character-at-judgment-filthy-still-righteous-still` тАФ["he that is filthy shall be filthy still; and he that is righteous shall be righteous still; he that is happy shall be happy still; and he that is unhappy shall be unhappy still"; the fixity of character (Rev 22:11; 2 Ne 9:16) тАФ at some point what we have BECOME is set, the self built across a lifetime of choices is the self we carry into eternity; not that God refuses to change the filthy but that the day comes when the filthy no longer WILL to be changed, character hardened into permanence; why "be wise in the days of your probation" is urgent тАФ probation is the days the soul is still soft enough to be remade]тЖТ 9:14 (Rev 22:11; 2 Ne 9:16; Alma 34:34-35; D&C 88:35)
- `doctrine:condemn-not-the-records-imperfections-give-thanks-and-be-wiser` тАФ["Condemn me not because of mine imperfection, neither my father... but rather GIVE THANKS unto God that he hath made manifest unto you our imperfections, that ye may learn to be more wise than we have been"; an astonishing thing for a writer of scripture to say тАФ he doesn't claim perfection, acknowledges the imperfections, and asks the reader not merely to forgive but to be GRATEFUL for them, because they're instructive: see what we got wrong and be wiser; the flaws are not a defect to apologize away but a gift; warmer than 8:17 тАФ "give thanks for the imperfections"; the humility of a man who knows the treasure is the truth not the polish, and trusts God to carry truth through the imperfect vessel]тЖТ 9:31-34 (Mormon 8:17; Ether 12:23-28; 3 Ne 5:18; 1 Ne 19:6)
- `theme:the-book-closes-on-the-covenant-not-the-destruction` тАФ["these things are written that we may rid our garments of the blood of our brethren, who have dwindled in unbelief... may God the Father remember the covenant which he hath made with the house of Israel; and may he bless them forever, through faith on the name of Jesus Christ. Amen"; the watchman's discharge (Ezek 3:18-19, 2 Ne 9:44) тАФ the prophet who warns has cleared his garments, the duty is to testify whatever the people do; the final words of the book of Mormon are not about its writers or readers but about the COVENANT тАФ the book that began with a family leaving Jerusalem and ends with the last man of their posterity writing alone in the ruins closes not on the destruction but on the covenant that outlasts the fall (Morm 5:20); from the ashes a blessing, from the dust a prayer for the future]тЖТ 9:35-37 (Ezek 3:18-19; 2 Ne 9:44; Morm 5:20; Rom 11:25-29)

## тАФ THE BOOK OF ETHER (the Jaredite record, abridged by Moroni) тАФ

### from Ether 1
- `doctrine:Ether-is-a-second-independent-witness-the-same-covenant-the-same-rise-and-fall` тАФ[the Jaredites are a WHOLE SEPARATE civilization that left the Old World at the great tower (Babel, ~2200 BC), 1500+ years before Lehi, and came to THIS SAME LAND and rose and fell here before the Nephites; that a second civilization unknown to history lived and died on the promised land reframes the BoM's central covenant тАФ the land "choice above all the lands of the earth" is not a one-time promise to one family but a RECURRING covenant offered across millennia on the same terms; Ether proves the BoM's central pattern is a LAW of the land тАФ consecrated, given to those who serve God, the wicked swept off; two civilizations, same covenant, same outcome, same warning to whoever holds the land next]тЖТ 1:1-5, 42 (1 Ne 2:20; Ether 2:7-12; 2 Ne 1:5-9; Mosiah 28:17-19)
- `doctrine:the-record-nested-three-deep-Moroni-abridging-Ether-recording-the-Jaredites` тАФ[a record nested three deep тАФ Moroni abridging Ether recording the Jaredites, a witness within a witness within a witness; from "the twenty and four plates which were found by the people of Limhi" (Mosiah 8, 21) and translated by King Mosiah (Mosiah 28); Moroni's editorial restraint тАФ he does NOT duplicate what is "had among the Jews" (creation-to-Babel, Genesis 1-11), gives only the part the world doesn't have ("from the tower down until they were destroyed"); a scribe who respects both his sources and his reader's time]тЖТ 1:1-6 (Mosiah 8:7-12; Mosiah 28:11-19; Alma 37:21-31; Gen 1-11)
- `doctrine:the-brother-of-Jared-the-intercessor-prayer-that-widens-to-include-others` тАФ[at the tower Jared turns to his brother тАФ "a large and mighty man, and a man highly favored of the Lord" тАФ "Cry unto the Lord, that he will not confound us"; Jared has the idea but asks his BROTHER to pray, the one whose prayers reach; the language is preserved by prayer; and the intercession WIDENS тАФ "Cry again... that he confound not their language" of their FRIENDS тАФ the brother of Jared doesn't stop at saving himself and Jared but prays for the friends too, and they're spared; true intercession doesn't stop at the self, it keeps widening (as Enos's did, Enos 1:9-11); the circle of mercy enlarges with the heart of the one who prays]тЖТ 1:34-37 (Enos 1:9-11; 3 Ne 17:14-21; Moses 7:18-21; Gen 18:23-32)
- `doctrine:the-Lord-had-compassion-the-God-of-justice-is-also-the-God-of-compassion` тАФ[three times in a few verses the Lord's response to the brother of Jared's crying is named as COMPASSION (vv35, 37, 40); the God of Ether is not a distant deity who confounds and scatters with cold sovereignty but One who "had compassion" the moment His servant cried; the same God who in His wrath swore the peoples would be scattered has compassion on the one who turns to Him IN the midst of that judgment; the judgment was real (languages confounded, peoples scattered) but never the whole of God тАФ the door to compassion stayed open for anyone who would cry]тЖТ 1:35, 37, 40 (Ex 34:6-7; Ps 86:15; Mosiah 15:9; Alma 26:37)
- `doctrine:faith-reaches-past-the-crisis-toward-the-promise-and-binds-itself-in-advance` тАФ["who knoweth but the Lord will carry us forth into a land which is choice above all the earth? And if it so be, LET US BE FAITHFUL unto the Lord, that we may receive it for our inheritance"; the brother of Jared's inquiries escalate тАФ from anxiety (will we be driven out?) to hope (might He lead us somewhere choice?) to commitment (let us be faithful, that we may receive it); faith reaches past the immediate crisis toward the promise, and binds itself to faithfulness IN ADVANCE of receiving; the Lord's answer matches the reach of the asking тАФ not merely "you won't be scattered" but a land, a nation, an inheritance]тЖТ 1:38-43 (1 Ne 3:7; Heb 11:8; Prov 3:5-6; Ether 12:4)
- `theme:the-choice-land-opened-because-this-long-time-ye-have-cried-unto-me` тАФ["thus I will do unto thee BECAUSE THIS LONG TIME YE HAVE CRIED UNTO ME"; the reason the Lord gives for the whole blessing тАФ not their worthiness in the abstract or their strength, but that they had cried unto Him over a long time; persistent prayer opened the choice land; the founding lesson of Ether laid down in its first chapter тАФ cry unto the Lord, keep crying, widen the prayer to include others, reach in faith past the crisis toward the promise, and the God of compassion will go before you into a land choice above all the earth]тЖТ 1:42-43 (Luke 18:1-8; Enos 1:12; 2 Ne 32:9; 3 Ne 27:28-29)

### from Ether 2
- `doctrine:the-choice-land-decree-serve-God-or-be-swept-off` тАФ["whoso should possess this land of promise, from that time henceforth and forever, should serve him, the true and only God, or they should be swept off when the fulness of his wrath should come upon them"; the consecration of the land sworn to the brother of Jared, binding "from that time henceforth and forever" on EVERY nation that would possess it, not just the Jaredites; the condition absolute and simple тАФ serve God or be swept off, no third option, no neutral tenancy; the land is holy ground tolerating only one kind of occupant; the explicit statement of the law the whole book of Ether demonstrates]тЖТ 2:7-10 (1 Ne 2:20; 2 Ne 1:5-9; Ether 9:20; Ether 13:2)
- `doctrine:the-sweeping-off-comes-only-when-iniquity-is-full-the-long-suffering-in-the-decree` тАФ["the fulness of his wrath cometh upon them when they are ripened in iniquity... it is not until the fulness of iniquity among the children of the land, that they are swept off"; the mercy folded into the severity тАФ God does not destroy at the first sin or the hundredth, He waits until the iniquity is FULL (Gen 15:16, the Amorites' iniquity "not yet full"); the long-suffering built into the decree; the Jaredites and Nephites both proved how much wickedness God will bear before the fulness comes; the judgment is real and certain but never hasty]тЖТ 2:9-10 (Gen 15:16; 1 Ne 14:6; 2 Ne 28:16; Hel 13:38)
- `doctrine:national-freedom-is-conditioned-on-serving-the-God-of-the-land-who-is-Jesus-Christ` тАФ["this cometh unto you, O ye Gentiles... that ye may repent... whatsoever nation shall possess it shall be free from bondage, and from captivity, and from all other nations under heaven, IF THEY WILL BUT SERVE the God of the land, WHO IS JESUS CHRIST"; the decree turned on US тАФ two civilizations already swept off for ripening in iniquity, the latter-day Gentiles under the identical decree; freedom (national liberty, freedom from captivity and other nations) conditioned on serving Christ тАФ a startling claim about the link between a nation's righteousness and its liberty; and the God of the land named by name: Jesus Christ (the God of the OT land-covenant is Christ)]тЖТ 2:11-12 (1 Ne 13:19; Mosiah 29:32; D&C 101:79-80; 2 Ne 1:7)
- `doctrine:even-the-favored-neglect-prayer-the-three-hour-chastening` тАФ["the Lord... chastened him because he remembered not to call upon the name of the Lord"; the brother of Jared тАФ "highly favored," the great intercessor whose prayers preserved the language тАФ had stopped praying, apparently for FOUR YEARS at the seashore, and the Lord chastened him three hours; spiritual favor is NOT immunity from spiritual drift тАФ the man who could move mountains by prayer let his prayers lapse and needed a rebuke to call him back; but mercy even in the chastening тАФ the Lord "talked with" him three hours, the rebuke inside a conversation, the correction itself a return to the voice he'd neglected]тЖТ 2:14 (1 Ne 16:25; Heb 12:5-11; Rev 3:19; Hel 12:3)
- `doctrine:the-Spirit-will-not-always-strive-with-man` тАФ["my Spirit will not always strive with man; wherefore, if ye will sin until ye are fully ripe ye shall be cut off from the presence of the Lord"; the same principle running through this closing section тАФ the day of grace passing (Morm 2:15), the gifts ceasing (Morm 9:20), the Spirit ceasing to strive (Morm 5:16); the striving is patient but not infinite; the chastening was a mercy precisely because it came WHILE the Spirit was still striving тАФ before the ripeness, while there was still time to be called back]тЖТ 2:15 (Gen 6:3; 2 Ne 26:11; Morm 5:16; Morm 9:20)
- `doctrine:God-answers-prayer-with-a-question-what-will-ye-that-I-should-do` тАФ[the brother of Jared came with two problems (no air, no light); the Lord solves the AIR directly ("make a hole in the top, and also in the bottom"), but for the LIGHT He turns the question back тАФ "What will ye that I should do that ye may have light in your vessels?" тАФ first ruling out the obvious answers (windows would shatter, fire is impossible in a sealed tossing vessel), then "what will ye that I should prepare for you?"; God's response was a QUESTION, not because He lacked an answer but because He wanted the man to bring one; He requires the brother of Jared to think, use his agency and reason, PROPOSE something, then bring it to God to be sanctified (D&C 9:8, study it out then ask); God often refuses to do FOR us what He's prepared us to do WITH Him; the unanswered half of the prayer was the invitation to a greater faith тАФ the shining stones of ch 3 possible only because God first declined to solve it Himself]тЖТ 2:18-25 (D&C 9:7-9; Matt 7:7; 1 Ne 17:50-51; Ether 3:1-6)

### from Ether 3
- `doctrine:faith-and-works-meet-man-does-his-part-God-does-what-only-God-can` тАФ[the brother of Jared answers "what will ye that I should do?" by going to WORK тАФ climbs the mountain, molds sixteen clear stones out of solid rock, brings God a finished proposal; but asks God only to TOUCH them, the one thing only God can do (make them shine); the exact division of labor in all faithful action тАФ do everything within your power, ask God only for what is beyond it; God wouldn't do for him what he could do for himself, so he did it, and then God did the part that was His alone; faith is not the abdication of effort but effort offered to God for the touch that completes it; the stones are useless until God touches them, but God won't touch stones the man was unwilling to make]тЖТ 3:1-5 (Ether 2:23-25; D&C 9:7-9; 1 Ne 17:50-51; Jas 2:17-22)
- `doctrine:humility-about-self-and-boldness-about-God-are-the-two-halves-of-faith` тАФ["do not be angry with thy servant because of his weakness... we are unworthy before thee; because of the fall our natures have become evil continually" + "I know, O Lord, that thou hast all power... thou canst do this"; profound humility and astonishing boldness held together тАФ utterly humble about HIMSELF (fallen, weak, unworthy), utterly confident about GOD (all power); not in tension but the two halves of real faith; the man who thinks well of himself won't ask boldly (thinks he can manage), the man who thinks poorly of God won't either (doubts God will); only one honest about his nothingness AND certain of God's omnipotence prays like this тАФ his weakness no barrier to boldness because the boldness rests on God not himself]тЖТ 3:2-5 (Mosiah 3:19; Moses 1:10; Heb 4:16; 2 Cor 12:9-10)
- `doctrine:I-am-Jesus-Christ-I-am-the-Father-and-the-Son-the-premortal-Christs-self-declaration` тАФ["Behold, I am he who was prepared from the foundation of the world to redeem my people. Behold, I am Jesus Christ. I am the Father and the Son. In me shall all mankind have life... and they shall become my sons and my daughters"; the PREMORTAL Christ тАФ centuries before Bethlehem тАФ declaring His own name and nature; He names Himself "Jesus Christ" before being born under that name; calls Himself "the Father and the Son" (Abinadi's doctrine, Mosiah 15:2-5 тАФ Son by His flesh, Father by being creator + divine investiture, one Being in whom the wills are perfectly one); claims the life of all mankind; FOUNDATIONAL text for whether Jesus is God тАФ the premortal Lord declares Himself God, names Himself Christ, claims the Father-and-Son identity; one of the two passages (with Mosiah 15 + the larger Ether vision) the is-jesus-christ-god answer rests on]тЖТ 3:14 (Mosiah 15:1-5; Mosiah 3:8; Alma 11:38-39; D&C 93:3-4)
- `doctrine:the-imago-Dei-man-created-after-the-body-of-Gods-spirit` тАФ["Seest thou that ye are created after mine own image? Yea, even all men were created in the beginning after mine own image. Behold, this body, which ye now behold, is the body of my spirit; and man have I created after the body of my spirit; and even as I appear unto thee to be in the spirit will I appear unto my people in the flesh"; the imago Dei stated more directly than anywhere else тАФ the brother of Jared sees Christ's SPIRIT BODY, in the form of a man because man is created in the form of God; Genesis 1:26 ("in our image") given its fullest commentary тАФ the likeness real and physical; the same form Christ shows in the spirit He'll show "in the flesh" (the Incarnation foreseen); the vision reveals who Christ is (God in the form of man) and who man is (made in the form of God)]тЖТ 3:15-16 (Gen 1:26-27; Mosiah 7:27; D&C 20:17-18; Moses 6:9)
- `doctrine:that-this-man-might-know-that-he-was-God` тАФ[Moroni's narrator-testimony тАФ "Jesus showed himself unto this man in the spirit... and he ministered unto him even as he ministered unto the Nephites; and all this, THAT THIS MAN MIGHT KNOW THAT HE WAS GOD"; the narrator's own declaration of Christ's divinity тАФ the whole vision given so the brother of Jared would KNOW Jesus is God; another foundational is-jesus-christ-god datapoint тАФ Moroni, narrating, says of Jesus "that he was God"]тЖТ 3:17-18 (3 Ne 11:8-16; Moses 1:2; John 14:9; Ether 4:7)
- `doctrine:faith-perfected-becomes-knowledge-and-cannot-be-kept-from-within-the-veil` тАФ["because of the knowledge of this man he could not be kept from beholding within the veil... he had faith no longer, for he knew, nothing doubting. Wherefore, having this perfect knowledge of God, he could not be kept from within the veil; therefore he saw Jesus"; faith perfected INTO knowledge тАФ the brother of Jared's faith so complete ("nothing doubting") it ceased to be faith and became knowledge (Alma 32:34, perfect knowledge makes faith dormant); the stunning consequence тАФ the veil is NOT a wall God erects to keep us out but a function of our unbelief, and when faith becomes perfect knowledge the veil cannot hold; he didn't break through by force or special permission, he simply believed so completely there was nothing left for the veil to do; the veil thins exactly to the degree doubt dissolves]тЖТ 3:19-20 (Alma 32:34; Ether 12:19-21; Heb 11:1; 2 Cor 5:7)
- `doctrine:faith-that-God-CAN-show-all-things-unlocks-all-things` тАФ["he showed unto the brother of Jared all the inhabitants of the earth which had been, and also all that would be... if he would believe in him that he could show unto him all thingsтАФit should be shown unto him; therefore the Lord could not withhold anything from him, for he knew that the Lord could show him all things"; the panoramic vision of all history (like Moses 1:8, Enoch, Nephi); the faith that God CAN show all things is the faith that unlocks all things тАФ the brother of Jared saw everything because he believed without limit that God was able; "the Lord COULD NOT withhold" тАФ faith that complete leaves God nothing to withhold]тЖТ 3:25-26 (Moses 1:8; 2 Ne 27:7-11; 1 Ne 14:24-26; Ether 4:4)
- `theme:the-sealed-record-and-the-interpreters` тАФ["thou shalt not suffer these things... to go forth unto the world, until the time cometh that I shall glorify my name in the flesh... ye shall write them and shall seal them up... in a language that they cannot be read... these two stones will I give unto thee... I will cause in my own due time that these stones shall magnify to the eyes of men these things which ye shall write"; the origin of the sealed portion of the plates (2 Ne 27) and of the instruments (the interpreters / Urim and Thummim, Mosiah 8:13, D&C 17) by which Joseph Smith would translate; the vision written, sealed in a confounded language, and the two stones provided to magnify it in due time]тЖТ 3:21-28 (Mosiah 8:13-18; 2 Ne 27:6-23; D&C 17:1; JS-H 1:35)

### from Ether 4
- `doctrine:the-greater-things-wait-on-the-greater-faith-faith-like-the-brother-of-Jared` тАФ["they shall not go forth unto the Gentiles until the day that they shall repent... and in that day that they shall exercise faith in me... even as the brother of Jared did... then will I manifest unto them the things which the brother of Jared saw, even to the unfolding unto them all my revelations"; the brother of Jared's full vision тАФ the GREATEST things ever made manifest тАФ is sealed, the condition for release being the same faith he had; the greater things wait on a CAPACITY perfect faith creates; the sealed portion (2 Ne 27) is locked not by God's reluctance but by our unreadiness тАФ the two-thirds Joseph couldn't translate remain sealed because no one has yet exercised faith enough to receive them]тЖТ 4:6-7 (Ether 3:9-20; 2 Ne 27:7-11; 3 Ne 26:9-11; Alma 32:34)
- `doctrine:Jesus-Christ-the-Son-of-God-the-Father-of-heaven-and-earth-I-am-the-light-and-the-life-and-the-truth` тАФ["saith Jesus Christ, the Son of God, the Father of the heavens and of the earth, and all things that in them are"; and "he that will not believe my words will not believe meтАФthat I AM... For behold, I am the Father, I am the light, and the life, and the truth of the world"; Christ as Son of God AND Father of heaven and earth (Creator), the doubled identity of Ether 3:14 + Mosiah 15; the great "I AM" gathering the Johannine sayings (John 8:12 "light of the world", John 14:6 "the way, the truth, and the life", John 8:58 "before Abraham was, I am") in the mouth of the premortal Christ; is-jesus-christ-god datapoints]тЖТ 4:7, 12 (Ether 3:14; Mosiah 15:1-5; John 8:58; John 14:6)
- `doctrine:whatsoever-persuades-men-to-do-good-is-of-Christ-the-Spirit-confirms-truth-by-persuading-to-good` тАФ["because of my Spirit he shall know that these things are true; for it persuadeth men to do good. And whatsoever thing persuadeth men to do good is of me; for good cometh of none save it be of me. I am the same that leadeth men to all good"; the test the whole BoM hands the reader, given here by Christ Himself тАФ the Spirit confirms truth by PERSUADING TO GOOD, whatever persuades to good is of God (same logic as Moro 7:16-17, Moro 10:4-5); a working criterion тАФ not abstract proof but the DIRECTION a thing pulls the soul; the BoM's claim to truth and its claim to goodness are the same claim]тЖТ 4:11-12 (Moro 7:16-17; Moro 10:4-5; Omni 1:25; Alma 5:40)
- `doctrine:rend-that-veil-of-unbelief-the-veil-is-ours-not-Gods` тАФ["when ye shall REND THAT VEIL OF UNBELIEF which doth cause you to remain in your awful state of wickedness, and hardness of heart, and blindness of mind, then shall the great and marvelous things which have been hid up from the foundation of the world... be made manifest... it hath not come unto you, because of unbelief"; the doctrine of Ether 3:19-20 turned into a commandment to the reader тАФ the veil between us and the greater things is OUR OWN unbelief, and the verb is active: REND it; the veil is not something God places to keep us out but something we maintain and are commanded to tear; humbling (the obstacle is in us) and electrifying (the veil is rendable, the brother of Jared's access open to anyone whose faith becomes what his was) at once]тЖТ 4:13-15 (Ether 3:19-20; 2 Cor 3:14-16; Heb 10:19-22; D&C 38:8)
- `doctrine:the-veil-is-rent-by-a-broken-heart-and-a-contrite-spirit` тАФ["when ye shall call upon the Father in my name, with a broken heart and a contrite spirit, then shall ye know that the Father hath remembered the covenant"; the veil of unbelief is rent not by intellectual achievement but by the humbled, contrite approach to God тАФ the same broken heart and contrite spirit that is the only sacrifice Christ asks (3 Ne 9:20); the brother of Jared's "exceeding faith" and our "broken heart and contrite spirit" are the same key in different hands тАФ both the posture of a soul that has stopped doubting and come to God with nothing held back]тЖТ 4:15 (3 Ne 9:20; Ps 51:17; 3 Ne 12:19; Ether 12:27)
- `theme:the-records-coming-forth-is-the-sign-the-work-of-the-Father-has-commenced` тАФ["when ye shall receive this record ye may know that the work of the Father has commenced upon all the face of the land"; the same sign Mormon and Moroni keep naming (3 Ne 29:1, Morm 8:35) тАФ the book's arrival is the evidence the gathering has begun; the chapter ties the coming-forth of the record to the gathering and closes on the same simple gospel call that closed book after book тАФ "repent all ye ends of the earth, and come unto me, and believe in my gospel, and be baptized"; the sealed vision and the open invitation hang on the same hinge: faith enough to come to Christ with nothing held back]тЖТ 4:16-19 (3 Ne 21:1-7; Morm 8:35; 3 Ne 29:1; 3 Ne 27:20)

### from Ether 5
- `doctrine:Moroni-addresses-the-translator-directly-the-writers-were-shown-their-readers` тАФ[Moroni stops narrating the Jaredites and speaks DIRECTLY to the man who would translate his words тАФ Joseph Smith, 1400 years away: "touch them not in order that ye may translate"; the pronoun singular and personal тАФ YE who will translate; Moroni knew there'd be a translator, addressed him by his task, gave an instruction (leave the sealed portion) Joseph would obey; same intimacy as Morm 8:35 тАФ the writers shown the future and writing into it, a letter to known recipients; Moroni is the angel who'd stand in Joseph's room and deliver these very plates, here writing to that future encounter as though already underway]тЖТ 5:1 (Morm 8:34-35; 2 Ne 27:6-22; D&C 3:16; Ether 4:5)
- `doctrine:the-law-of-witnesses-three-men-plus-the-fourfold-divine-testimony` тАФ["unto three shall they be shown by the power of God... in the mouth of three witnesses shall these things be established; and the testimony of three, and this work, in the which shall be shown forth the power of God and also his word, of which the Father, and the Son, and the Holy Ghost bear record"; the prophecy of the Three Witnesses (Oliver/David/Martin, D&C 17), resting on the ancient law (Deut 19:15, 2 Cor 13:1); God doesn't ask belief on Joseph's word alone but establishes truth in the mouth of witnesses; and MORE than three named тАФ the three men, the work itself, the power of God, the word, and the Father+Son+Holy Ghost bearing record; the human witnesses the legal minimum, the divine witnesses the real foundation; the threefold divine witness here is the same Godhead confessed as "one God" (Morm 7:7), seen from the side of their unified testimony]тЖТ 5:2-4 (2 Ne 27:12-14; D&C 17:1-5; Deut 19:15; Morm 7:7)
- `doctrine:the-testimony-stands-against-the-world-at-the-last-day-but-the-door-is-open` тАФ["all this shall stand as a testimony against the world at the last day... and if it so be that they repent and come unto the Father in the name of Jesus, they shall be received into the kingdom of God"; the witnesses are not only for the believer's comfort but evidence in the final judgment тАФ a record so abundantly witnessed leaves the world without excuse; to reject a testimony established by the law of witnesses and sealed by the Godhead is to be judged by it; but the door is open тАФ the testimony that stands AGAINST the world is the same that, received, brings a soul INTO the kingdom; the evidence cuts both ways depending on what the reader does with it]тЖТ 5:4-5 (2 Ne 25:18; 3 Ne 27:25-26; Morm 9:27; Moro 10:30-32)
- `doctrine:Moroni-stakes-his-authority-on-meeting-the-reader-at-the-judgment` тАФ["if I have no authority for these things, judge ye; for ye shall know that I have authority when ye shall see me, and we shall stand before God at the last day. Amen"; not the hedging of a man unsure of his ground тАФ Moroni puts his own authority on the table and tells the reader you'll find out whether I had it when you MEET ME, for we'll stand before God together at the judgment; a claim only makeable by someone certain he'll be there, the reader will be there, and the meeting will vindicate him; for Joseph Smith literal тАФ he DID see Moroni face to face; for the rest of us future, but Moroni writes as one who will personally meet every reader at the bar of God and answer for what he wrote тАФ a bracing accountability, not an anonymous ancient voice but a man who'll look his readers in the eye at the judgment]тЖТ 5:6 (Moro 10:27; 2 Ne 33:11; Jacob 6:13; Moro 10:34)

### from Ether 6
- `doctrine:the-storm-that-buries-them-is-the-wind-that-drives-them-home` тАФ[God does not give calm seas but "a furious wind"; they are "many times buried in the depths of the sea, because of the mountain waves... and the great and terrible tempests" тАФ BURIED, submerged again and again; yet the same wind that buries does the one thing they need: "the wind did never cease to blow TOWARDS THE PROMISED LAND while they were upon the waters"; one of the most important pictures of affliction in scripture тАФ the storm that nearly drowns them is the very thing driving them home; God didn't calm the wind, He AIMED it; the affliction itself was not an obstacle to the journey but the means of it; sometimes the storm is not the enemy of your journey but its engine, the same wind that buries you blowing you home]тЖТ 6:5-8 (Ether 2:24-25; 1 Ne 18:8-13; Ps 107:23-30; Rom 8:28)
- `doctrine:praise-all-the-day-long-in-the-storm-gratitude-in-the-tempest` тАФ["he did thank and praise the Lord all the day long; and when the night came, they did not cease to praise the Lord"; buried in the deep, tossed by mountain waves, in a sealed barge for the better part of a year тАФ and the response is PRAISE, not complaint, not the murmuring Laman and Lemuel offered in their storm (1 Ne 18:9); the same man chastened three chapters ago for NEGLECTING prayer for four years (2:14) now will not stop praising; the transformation complete; he can praise in the storm because he understands what it's doing тАФ carrying them home; gratitude in the tempest is faith that it's in God's hand and aimed at the promise]тЖТ 6:9-10 (1 Ne 18:9-16; Ps 34:1-3; Mosiah 26:39; Ether 2:14)
- `doctrine:the-light-God-gives-holds-even-under-the-waves` тАФ["they did have light continually, whether it was above the water or under the water"; the stones God touched shone even in the depths тАФ the light He gave did not fail when they were submerged; the light held under the waves; so does His presence тАФ the faith-light that carries through the storm doesn't go out when you're buried in it]тЖТ 6:10 (Ether 3:4-6; D&C 88:11-13; John 1:5; Ps 139:11-12)
- `theme:the-journey-through-the-storm-ends-in-worship-and-tears-of-joy` тАФ["when they had set their feet upon the shores of the promised land they bowed themselves down upon the face of the land, and did humble themselves before the Lord, and did shed tears of joy before the Lord, because of the multitude of his tender mercies over them"; 344 days on the water (echoing Noah's flood) and the first act on solid ground is WORSHIP тАФ bowing, humbling, weeping for joy at God's "tender mercies" (the phrase Nephi opened with, 1 Ne 1:20); the journey through the storm ends not in relief or self-congratulation but in tears of gratitude; the people who praised through the tempest now weep with thanksgiving on the shore]тЖТ 6:11-12 (1 Ne 1:20; Ps 116:12-14; Gen 8:13-20; Alma 26:8)
- `doctrine:surely-this-thing-leadeth-into-captivity-the-anti-monarchy-warning` тАФ[the people ask to anoint a king, and the brother of Jared's response is immediate and grieved: "this was grievous unto them... Surely this thing leadeth into captivity"; the same anti-monarchy wisdom Samuel gave Israel (1 Sam 8:10-18) and Mosiah built his reform on (Mosiah 29) тАФ a king concentrates power in one fallible man, the people's liberty hostage to his righteousness; the brother of Jared sees at the very founding where it leads, and the ENTIRE book of Ether is the proof тАФ the Jaredite kings dethroning/imprisoning/murdering one another across generations, the people repeatedly in captivity; he saw it on day one, but Jared overruled him]тЖТ 6:22-24 (1 Sam 8:10-18; Mosiah 23:7-13; Mosiah 29:16-23; Ether 7:5)
- `doctrine:kingship-cannot-be-forced-constrain-no-man-to-be-your-king` тАФ[Pagag, the firstborn chosen king, "refused and would not be their king"; the people would that his father constrain him, "but his father would not; and he commanded them that they should constrain no man to be their king"; even the king must CONSENT тАФ the office cannot be imposed; one bright detail in the founding of a monarchy that will lead to captivity тАФ at least the throne is not forced on an unwilling man]тЖТ 6:25-27 (Mosiah 29:38-39; D&C 121:39; 2 Cor 9:7; Philem 1:14)
- `theme:a-good-first-king-delays-but-does-not-remove-the-structural-danger` тАФ[Orihah, the first king, is righteous тАФ he "did walk humbly before the Lord, and did remember how great things the Lord had done for his father, and also taught his people"; the institution begins well, with a good man who remembers and teaches; but the warning "this thing leadeth into captivity" stands over the whole book like a shadow тАФ a good first king does not undo the structural danger of concentrated power, it only delays it; the Jaredites will spend the rest of Ether proving the brother of Jared right]тЖТ 6:28-30 (Mosiah 29:25-32; Hel 5:2; 1 Sam 8:9; Eccl 8:9)
